dānam vipraṇaśyati śrāṃtāya a dṛṣṭa pūrvāya ati annam adhva nivarti ne yaḥ udayāt aparikliṣṭam sa samṛddhim avāpnuyāt pitṝn devān tathā viprān atithīn śva mahā mune pramucyate brāhmaṇyeṣu akṣayam dānam annam śūdre mahat phalam anna pānam ca śūdre ca bāhmaṇe ca viśiṣyate na pṛcchet gotra caraṇam svādhyāyam deśam eva ca bhikṣite brāhmaṇena i ha dadyāt annam prayācataḥ anna dsi aśubha vṛkṣāḥ sarva kāma phala anvitāḥ bhavanti iha yathā putra harṣa yuktāḥ triviṣṭape mahā mune bhavanāni prakāśante divi teṣām mahātmanām nānā saṃsthāna rūpāṇi nānā kāma anvitāni ca sarva kāmaphala aśvā piṭakṣā vyāsaḥ uvāca tapasaḥ me phalam būhi punar eva viśeṣataḥ pravakṣyāmi tapodhyāyam sarva kāma artha sādhakam su duśvaram dvijātīnām tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu tapasā a prāpyate svargaḥ tapasā a prāpyate yaśaḥ pāpa haram śivam kumāraḥ sarva lokānām namaskṛtyam pitāmaham provāca idam mahā ākhyānam devarṣiḥ brahma sūnunā gataḥ aham dharmarājānam draṣṭum sam pūjitaḥ umayā mayā tatra upaviṣṭena dṛṣṭam kiṃcid mahā adbhutam kāṃcanena vimānena vaiḍūrya tavedinā maṇi muktā vicitreṇa kiṃkiṇī jāla śobhinā āgatam puruṣam tatra āsanāt devam sattamaḥ sa saṃbhramam samutthāya dṛṣṭvā adharmaḥ svayam vikṣuḥ gṛhītvā idam tadā vākyam uvāca samīpe mama tiṣṭhasva yāvat ājñā sata āgataḥ puruṣaḥ divyaḥ yatra tiṣṭhati dharmarāj svayam dharmeṇa vai brahman vā apūjām kṛtāṃtayoḥ tatra me vismayaḥ jātaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ umayā tatas naraḥ tava sakāśam hiyaḥ yaṃ pūrvam iha āgataḥ kim anena kṛtam karma yasi atuṣṭaḥ bhavān bhṛśam tathā eva āsyaka tā pūjāḥ yaḥ tvam ābhyām samam pūjām kuruṣe dharma kāraṇāt brahma viṣṇu śiva ādyaiḥ va pūjyase tvam sadā bhṛśam kṛtam śubham iha āyāti itat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate vaidiśam nāma nagaram pṛthivyām asti viśrutam tatra abhūt pṛthivīpālaḥ dharāpāla eti śrutaḥ kasmin kāle purā devī śaśāpa sva gaṇam kudhā rī bhartuḥ yat maniveśi tā tasmāt dādaśa varṣāṇi jaṃbukaḥ tvam bhaviṣyasi tatra asau aśanam kṛtvā kṣetretrāṇān tatas asṭajat tatra āśvaryam mahat ṛṣṭvā adharāpālaḥ mahīpatiḥ śaṃbhoḥ āyatanam kṛtvā āsthāpayāmāsa vaiśivam śubham āyatanam śaṃbhoḥ tasmin agre sabhājanaiḥ pūrṇetu brāhmaṇa ādīnām pūjayitvā kadaṃbakam itihāsa purāṇa jña vācakam ca viśeṣataḥ pūjayitvā dija śreṣṭham vidyāśreṣṭham mahā munim pustakam ca api saṃpūjya gaṃdha puṣpa ādibhiḥ kramāt tatas tam āha rājā asau uvāca kaṃ vinaya anvitaḥ mayā iha āyatanam śaṃbhoḥ kāritam tu śiva agratas cāturvarṇyam idam ca api śrotu kāmam kadaṃbakam tiṣṭhati iha dvijaśreṣṭha kuru pustaka vācanam svarṇa niṣka śatam ca atra tatodāsye tathā aparam pūrṇevarṣe a dvija śreṣṭha śreyaḥ artham aham ātmanaḥ atha āyuṣaḥ kṣayāt ca ayam kāladharmam upeyivān mayā ācātsya vimānam hiśivena preritam divi iti eṣā a karmaṇā uthyuṣṭiḥ puṇya ākhyānaka saṃjñikā gaṃdha puṣpa upahāraiḥ tu na tuṣṭiḥ jāyate tathā devānām iha sarveṣām purāṇa śravaṇā yathā go suvarṇa hiraṇyānām vastrāṇām ca api kṛtsraśas grāmāṇām nagarāṇām ca dānāt tuṣṭiḥ bhavet na hi yathā asyāt dharma śravaṇāt prītiḥ sarva divaukasām itihāsa purāṇānām śravaṇam muni sattama yathā me syāt mahā trītiḥ na śrāddhaiḥ sarvakāmikaiḥ yaḥ ca ayam aparām vipra ehā āyātaḥ nara uttamaḥ saṃgatyā atugataḥ ca ayam dharma śravaṇam uttamam śrutvā abhaktiḥ abhūt asya tataśva śraddhayā anvitaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇa aṃtasya vācakasya mahātmanaḥ eṣa vipraḥ muni śreṣṭha pradadau svarṇa māṣakam na anya dānakadācakra lobha āviṣṭena cetasā pātra dāna phalāt eṣa prāptavān brahmaṇaḥ padam yat anena rutā pūjā vācakasya mahātmanaḥ tena aham pūjitaḥ sya vaii kavi ṣṇu śaṃkaraḥ tathā śrāddhe haṃ pūjitaḥ sya vai i daśa varṣāṇi paṃca ca kṛtsraśas devatānām ca aiṃdra ādīnām tathā bhavet brahma viṣṇu śiva ādīnām saṃdeṣṭā vācakaḥ umune prīte tasmin devatāḥ syuḥ sarvāḥ prītāḥ na saṃśayaḥ caṃdra āditya agraha ādayaḥ mad sādhanāya pūjyaṃte tatas saṃpūjyatām gatāḥ snānam pūjā japaḥ homaḥ śrutam śaucam ahiṃsa tā dhī biṃdya asatyam akrodhaḥ dānam kṣāṃtiḥ dayā damaḥ vāpī kūpa taḍāgānām prāsādānām ca kalpanam kṛcchra cāṃdrāyaṇam yajñāḥ tīrthāni sva āśramāṇi ca mad sādhanāni sarvāṇi proktāni iha manīṣibhiḥ duḥkham pāpāt vijānīhi tasmāt dharma mayam sukham trividham tam vijānīhi sattva rājasa tāmasam sadā satvam tapaḥ vidyāt muni siddheṣu nityaśas etat dṛṣṭvā āca śrutvā śyāśam iha āgataḥ śrutvā kumāra vacanam āha lokapitāmahaḥ yau dṛṣṭaubhavatātau tupurāṇau puṇyakāriṇau sūryeṇa api yat uktam hi tathyam vā enān yathā bhavet yadā āsīt me mukham putra paṃcamaṃloka pūjitam tasmāt etāni sarvāṇi niḥ sṛtāni samaṃtataḥ itihāsa purāṇāni lokānām hita kāmyayā yathā etāni mama iṣṭāni purāṇāni sadā mune na tathā caturaḥ ve dāna ca aṃgāni mahāmate dadātu uvāca keṭatti nityam śraddhā samanvitaḥ śṛṇvaṃti tāni ye bhaktyā ate yānti paramām gatim itihāsa purāṇāni spaṣṭīkaraṇam uttamam dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām mayāḥ sṛṣṭāni suvrata itihāsa puraṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhayet ye ete caturaḥ veda a gūḍha arthāḥ satatam sthitāḥ atas tu etāni sṛṣṭāni baḥ dhāya eṣām mahā mune karoti yaḥ sadā bhaktyā sayā ati paramam padam kṛtvā tu dakṣiṇām taṃtra param brahma adhigacchati na āścarya pātra dānāt hi dāna pātram hi tatparam tīrthānām iva kedāram vratānām ca mahā vratam parvatānām yayā meruḥ pakṣiṇām garuḍaḥ yathā gaṃgā ca sarva saritām devaśreṣṭhaḥ yathā śivaḥ pātrāṇām api sarveṣām vācakaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ pūjitam sakalam tena jagat syāt na atra saṃśayaḥ aho ti dhanya tātasya dharma śravaṇa kāriṇaḥ dānam yat dadata utyartha puṇya tā vāca kāyave iti śrī śivapurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām śravaṇamāhātmyakathanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śastāni ghora dānāni mahā dānāni nityaśas pātrebhyaḥ tu pradeyāni ātmānam tārayaṃti te hiraṇya dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca gṛhṇatau tau pavitrāṇi tārayaṃti svamevatam etāni śreṣṭha dānāni sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate pṛthvī sarasvatī deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam annam tathā eva ca eṣa buddhiṃmataḥ yajñaḥ śraddhā pūtaḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ viśi staḥ sarva yajñebhyaḥ dadataḥ iti anasūyayā mahāghorāṇi vakṣyāmi trāhmaṇyam upahanyate pātrāṇi śṭaṇu kāleyat tyājyāni asmai dvinā āpadam mṛta śayyā ajinam kṛṣṇam pāpāt vikrayam ātmanaḥ cāṃḍālāt patitāt mlecchāt tathā ca ubhayatas mukhī tulāyām roha naṃdānam kurukṣetra pratigrahaḥ tilaiḥ āpūraṇam kṛṣṇaiḥ dānāni eva pṛthak daśa yaḥ tu ekam pratigṛhṇāti brāhmaṇaḥ jñāna durbalaḥ dātā paṃke yathā ākṣipya pādam aśmani tat tathā saṃyāti paramam lokam yāvat ābhūtasam plavam pravakṣyāmi gati ca eṣām pralobha athṛta cetasām saṃprāpya su mahā dānam yadī chet gatim ātmanaḥ rutvā arddhena tu kāryāṇi vadānyaḥ kurute sadā evam san vipra mukhyaḥ upi gatim śreṣṭhām prayāti hi kanakam ca tilāḥ nāgāḥ kanyā dāsī gṛhaṃrathaḥ maṇayaḥ kapilāca eva mahā dānāḥ gṛhītvā tāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇaḥ jñāna vid sadā vadānyam tārayet ca eva ātmānam cana saṃśayaḥ suvarṇa prathamam dānam suvarṇa dakṣiṇā aparā daśa pūrvān daśa parān ātmānam ca ekaviṃśakam apipā paśataṃru tvāt datvā vipreṣu tārayet suvarṇaye prayacchaṃti narāḥ śuddhena cetasā devatāḥ te prayacchaṃti samaṃtāt ditinaḥ śrutam tasmāt suvarṇa da tvāca dattāḥ syuḥ sarva devatāḥ agniḥ hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇaḥ ca hutāśanaḥ vandya bhāve ca kurvaṃti vahni sthānam sarva veda pramāṇa jña a veda śruti nidarśanāt a sūtam yat a vācyam ca duṣṭam hi pūta tām vrajet piḍha deva manuṣyāṇā miṣṭam tat sarvadā mune sarvam āpaḥ śuddhi vajaṃti hi hemnā tasmāt sadā śuddham hāṭakam vanhi saṃbhavam dadyāt vataṃsam uddiśya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt svarṇa daḥ sarva daḥ proktaḥ sarvān kāmān labhet divi vimānena arka varṇena bhāsvareṇa virājitaḥ apsaraḥ gaṇa kīrṇena gaṃdharva gati nādinā tasmāt sva śaktyā ādātavyam kāṃcanam mānavaiḥ bhuvi suvarṇaye prayacchaṃti narāḥ śuddhena cetasā vyāsaḥ uvāca bahu prakārāṇi mayā aśrutāni aho tvayā uktāni ityāni tāni śubhāni sarvāṇi viśeṣitāni pra brūhi dānam tvam atodharāyāḥ khyātam tvayā apūrvataraiḥ narādhipaiḥ dāna ādhipaiḥ sarva bhujaḥ babhūvuḥ tat eva dānam sarvam athonarāṇām tat te pravakṣyāmi kṛtam hiyena dāna uttamam tat tu adhu na āśṭaṇuṣva atra eva udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam rājā acitrarathaḥ nāma purā āsīt nṛpa sattamaḥ bubhuje saka lān bhogān sana dvīpavatīm mahīm tatra jitvā sahasrākṣam devaiḥ sārddham balāt tatas śāsanam kārayāmāsa svakīyam tatra tatra ha su vismayam abhūt tatra dṛṣṭvā rājyam sukham svakam putrāṇām ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi kośam ca akṣayam eva ca janānām anurāgam ca prabhūta vara vāhanam sphītiḥ jana par̤hānām cana akāla maraṇam tathā bhāryāyāḥ ca eva saubhāgyam rūpam ca apratimam tathā punar syāt iha saṃprāptiḥ pūrva dharmāt aham munīn pṛcchāmi sarva dharma jñān kariṣye sakalam punar evam saṃciṃtya rājā asau vasiṣṭham idam abravīt tvad prasādāt muni śreṣṭha rājyam avyāhatam bhuvi rūpam ca apratimam lokam bhāryā amesti su śobhanā śarīra ārogyam aiśvarya dāna śaktiḥ anuttamā su saṃtatiḥ su bhṛtya aśvasā anurāgā aśvame prajāḥ dharma hāni śvamena astiśaktiḥ mepālanebhuvaḥ sarvam kṛtāt dharmāt evam prāptam mayā akhilam tat śrutvā vacanam tasya vasiṣṭhaḥ prāhanaṃ nṛpam citayitvā aciram kālam śṭaṇu bhūpa anya janmani avaṃtī nagarī nāma pṛthivyā aja ghane sthitā dharmapālaḥ nṛpaḥ tatram sarva dharma anuśāsakaḥ vasataḥ te tu anādṛṣṭiḥ āsīt ca bahu vārṣikī anna kṣayāt tatas tvam tu gatvā ātuvanam āśrayat kṣudh kṣāma karṣitāḥ santaḥ phala mūla mahā āśinaḥ bhāryayā ayuktaḥ prāgāt aṃgāra kārakaḥ tasmāt tvam bhāryayā a yukta udārūṇyāt āyasa tvaraḥ prāviśat nagarīm sopi vikretu tāni sarvathā najagrāha janaḥ kaśvid aṃpatyoḥ aṭamānayoḥ tatas sāyam kṣudhā ārtau tau dhvanim śuśruvatuḥ tadā vaṇij mukhyasya viprāṇām javhata aṃta gṛha aṃgaṇe tau gatvā tatra kāṣṭhāḥ nijvālayāmāsatuḥ tadā samāgame rāvhanayoḥ mahābhāga tatratau ūṣatuḥ tadā palānām aṃśatame kasya samupoṣya janārdanam arcayitvā vidhānena vaṇij saḥ pi kṛta ādaraḥ sa abdhi dvīpavatīm rājan bhaktyā paramayā āyutaḥ sā adṛṣṭā vīyamānā vai yuvayoḥ kliśyamānayoḥ tam dṛṣṭvā aduḥkhasaṃta mauna kṛtam puṇyam āvayoḥ yena īdṛśau bhaviṣyāvaḥ dharaṃtau manasā tu iti prāpta adharma phalāt rājyam tasmāt tvam dehi sāṃpratam tasmāt tvam dehi rāja iṃdra pṛthivīm sarva kāma dām dīyamānām tra paśyaṃti pṛthvīm rukmasya bhaktitaḥ sarva pāpa vinirmuktāḥ teyāṃti paramām gatim śṛṇu bhūpāla bhardra temana sāyedharā pradāḥ sa abdhi dvīpavatīm dṛṣṭvā teṣām vākyam tathā tathā cakravartī mahā vīryaḥ pṛthū rāja adhipaḥ bhavat bubhuje pārthivam kṣetram sa deva asura rakṣasām svarga ca deva gaṃdharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ tat dattam ca upajīvaṃti tathā anye bhūbhṛtaḥ pica sarva ratna samāyuktam sapta dvīpavatīm mahīm śaśāsa dharmeṇa punar na adharmaḥ dṛśyate kutas na anyāya kṛt nava aśuddha ūna astenaḥ mūṣaka ādayaḥ dhanuṣkoṭi āruta ayenaniḥ adriḥ pṛthivīpurā tasya etat abhimānaṃca vīrya ca pṛthivīpateḥ rūpam dṛṣṭvā śubhā patnī tasya abhūt ca ati vismayā tatas sācita yāmāsa sammṛjya avismita asatī katham syāt saṃpad eṣām e kim punar aṃnya janmani evam sāva hudhā aciṃtya pṛthum ca eva samānudat tatas papraccha sarva jñān brāhmaṇān ādi bhūmipaḥ yadi sa anugrahā abuddhiḥ bhavatām muni sattamāḥ yathā vane su prasāditāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ yaḥ tam manasi saṃdehaḥ yaśva sāṃśayikaḥ bhuvi gadiṣyāmaḥ yathānyāyam tam pṛccha adya mahīpate saṃtuṣṭaḥ brāhmaṇa uśnīyāt śiyāt dām dha rma saṃśayam iti ukte prāhatān viprān ādirājā pṛthuḥ tadā kathayaṃtu yathāvṛttam kim mayā a su kṛtam kṛtam purā viprāḥ kiṃca anayā asu cāru aṃgyā mama patnyā arutam punar yena āvayoḥ iyam sphītiḥ su saṃbhūtā a su durlabhā catvāraḥ apratihata āgatayoḥ mama apṛcchataḥ śyāḥ kośasyām balam ca apratimam masti śarīra ārogyam uttamam sā ham icchāmi tam jñātum yathā ca iyam aniṃditā atibhāti cam ekāntyā bhāryā iyam atiśobhanā karma yasya aśeṣam idam phalam iti pṛṣṭāḥ nareṃdreṇa samastāḥ te tapodhanāḥ marīcim prerayāmāsuḥ kathyatām iti bhūpateḥ yogam āsthāya su ciram yathāvat ṛṣi sattamaḥ jñātavān ādirājasya sarva pūrva viceṣṭitam mahat ahata tobhūpam ciṃtita arthaḥ yata vrataḥ marīciḥ uvāca śṛṇu bhūpāla yasya idam sakalam karmaṇaḥ phalam babhūva tvam purā śūdraḥ para hiṃsā parāyaṇaḥ purā iyam bhavataḥ bhāryā pati trata parāyaṇā yadi niḥsvaḥ bhūtvā a parikṣīṇaḥ pareṣām bhṛtya tām gataḥ tyajyamānā api sā asādhu no tyaje ttvām aniṃditā sādhyā viṣṇoḥ āyatanetvayā nītā hema mayī pṛthvī dhaninaḥ vṛṣalasya tu ayodhyāyām mahā rājakasya bhaktyā anayā saha paricaryā kṛta a dātuḥ manasā apuṇya kāṃkṣiṇaḥ saṃmārjana ādikam sarva kṛtam te bhaktitaḥ nṛpa niḥśeṣam upaśātim tad pāpam śuśrūṣaṇāt anu sarva kāma pradam karma rukma dhenvāḥ kṛtam tvayā tena idam akhilam rājyam aśe ṣā jagatī tava evam nareṃdra śūdra tvāt tasya karma parāyaṇaḥ kim punar yaḥ naraḥ bhaktyā pṛthvīm haimīm prayacchati śatam pūrva aparam ca api kulānām tārayet nṛpa yāvat caṃdra śva sūryaḥ ca yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī idam yaḥ śṛṇuyāt nityam paṭhet ca eva iha bhaktitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca evam śrutvā sa rājā atu pṛthuḥ vainyaḥ pratāpavān yādṛśīm kārayāmāsa yad pramāṇām yad udbhavām paṃcaviśe hema mayyāḥ sa abdhi dvīpa yujaḥ bhuvaḥ svar upadāna māhātmyam yathāvat upavarṇyate ha mānava āloke śaktyā dātuḥ labhaṃti te lakṣaṇa suvarṇena sahasreṇa śatena tu suvarṇena tu kārayet eka hastām dvi hastām vā a tri hastām vā apikām atas hema abhāve su tāmrasya kṛtvā kṣipet ratna abhāvāt aṇuṣu eva haimam teṣu vinikṣipet gaṃdhamādana saṃjñam tu mero nīlaṃtu paścime bhāge vipula śva uttare tatas mahā paśu ime tad bhāvāt hiraṇyam tu mauktika ādi tatas param kadaṃba jaṃbuka aśvattha śrīpaṇa pallavam kramāt nāga vayāḥ tathā bhāvāt samyak patrāṇi vinyaset tena āpūrya tatas dvīpaḥ śālmali śvāparaḥ mune kuśadvīpāt parodanaḥ tena eva āpūrayet tatas krauṃcāt paraḥ tu dugdhena śākadvīpam atas param tasmāt tam madhunā āpūrya tad aṃte puṣkaram sthitam saṃkṣepāt kathitam vyāsa pṛthivī ādānam uttamam na asya a varṣa ayutena api vaktum śakya uti vistaraḥ hasta mātram khanet kuṃḍam homam tatra eva kārayet viṣṇostu tritayam hutvā āpaḥ deva iti anukramāt vasoḥ pavitram tritayam hutvāt nāvā hutīḥ tatas pṛthivi iti punar hutvā pūjayet tatra keśavam sarva āśrayaḥ tvam hi pumān aśeṣaḥ sṛṣṭā tvayā iyam pṛthivī dhṛtā a punar dātā tvam asyāḥ pratisaṃgrahītā tubhyam mayā hema mayī niveditā gṛhṇīṣva kāma abhimanaṃdadasva brāhmaṇān vācayitvā agre prīyatām dharaṇīdharaḥ evam datvā dvijebhyaḥ tān ṭaṇuka āle cayat phalam kulānām śatam āgāmi samatītam tathā śatam tārayitvā divam yāti yāvat iṃdrāḥ caturdaśa tatosāve kacchacaṃtu rājyam prāpnoti bhū tale kramāt mokṣam avāpnoti dānāt asyāḥ prabhāvataḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca saṃśayaḥ sarva tatva jñaḥ udānāt tvaṃbūhi pṛcchataḥ yat tat uktam purātena tat dānam būti aśeṣatas yena dānena sadyas nā pāpāt bhavati akilbiṣī yat sādhayet nirja deham kṛtvā pāpāni aśeṣa taḥ jīvam hi daihikāḥ deha saṃpīḍayā atābhyām naraḥ pāpāya mucyate tasmāt pṛccha ṛṣi śreṣṭha sāṃpratam kathayāmi te vyāsaḥ uvāca asmin kali yuge martyāḥ sat ācāra vivarjitāḥ bahu pāpa ratā mūḍhāḥ bhaviṣyaṃti mahā mune raurava ādipu ghorāṇām yātanāḥ kila śuśruma kāntāram gahanam tatra tad artham brūhima idvija yathā an apaśyet kāṃtāram su duṣpāram su durgamam sanatkumāraḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahā gu tyam mahāpātaka nāśanam kāṃtaram yena paśyaṃti tathā vakṣyāmi suvrata kārtikasya asite pakṣe caturdaśyām samāhitaḥ tila prastha mayam kṛtvā nāgam sarva guṇa anvitam dhenum vatsam suvarṇa tusu dīpaiḥ sarvatas citam suvarṇa tilaka upetam karṇa cāmara bhūṣitam kāṃsya ghaṃṭā yuga yutam kṣauma kakṣa vibhūṣitam mauktika āpūrṇa kuṃbhaṃtu siṃdūra avata mastakam vicitra vastra saṃvītam muktā mālā virājitam pādukā upānaham chatram bhājana āsana darpaṇam śaktyā kuryāt suvarṇena vitta śāṭhya vivarjitaḥ tasya agre iṣṭa dalam padmam saṃlikhet kuṃkuma ārutaiḥ āpūrya acyutam īśānam arcayet kaṇikā pade dhātāram viśva kartāram pūrva patre tu vāsavam namaḥ pitṛṇām pataye dharmāya ānaṃda dāyine namaḥ upāṃpataye tubhyam bhava bhīta ti hāriṇe namaḥ te pṛṣat aśvāya vāyave jagat āyuṣe namaḥ te paśu nāthāya śivāya īśāyate namaḥ kāṃtāra pataye dhātre trahmarudrāya viṣṇave viśvarūpāya devāya śarmadāya namaḥ namaḥ evam kalpa vidhānena tatra kāṃtāra devatāḥ devadevam tatas abhyarcya viṣṇum viśvapatim punar imam uccārayet maṃtram kṛta aṃjali puṭaḥ sudhīḥ kām tāram adhvanaḥ mārgam ibhena anena keśavaḥ ciṃtāmaṇiḥ tathā daṃtī sadā bhavatu mama vibho dadyāt rāhmaṇāya sva śaktitaḥ sa ratnam sa hiraṇyam ca sarva ābhara tatas naktam samaśnīyāt dīpam dadyāt tathā gaje pārthive rāja śārdūla kārtikyām vā pradāpayet hatvā a pāpāni aśeṣāṇi sa baṃdhuḥ samutsṛj janaḥ divisaṃkrīḍatevyāsa yāvat iṃdrāḥ caturdaśa kapilānām śate datte yat phalam jyeṣṭha puṣkare kāṃtārasya pradānena samaṃsyāt muni sattama kāṃtārasya pradānena tat phalam na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃnihatyām nara śreṣṭha rāḥ hu graste divākare dharā dānāt na tat puṇyam kāṃtāreṇa yat aśnute kṛṣṇājine nayat puṇyam bhūyas śataguṇena ca puṇyam tat sakalam labhyam mune kāntārahastinā gaja aśva ratha dhenūnām yat phalam hi nigadyate tat phalam sakalam vidyāt kāntāreṇa mahā mune tila ājya jala dhenūnām yat pūrva uktam phalam labhet tad mūrti tanmayīm da tvā apuṇyam śataguṇam labhet evam jñātvā muni śreṣṭha śreṣṭha kāṃtāra kāraṇam dadyāt anena maṃtreṇa saṃpūjya gaja puṃgavam namaḥ kāntāra rūpāya pa rameśāya śaṃbhave namaḥ uṣṭa diś ibha īśāya namaḥ rūpāya viplave anena tila kāntāra daṃti dānena daitya hā prīyatām puṃḍarīkākṣaḥ prabhuḥ kāṃtāra tārakaḥ evam uccārya tat dadyāt brāhmaṇāya kuṭuṃbine paṭhatām śṛṇva tām ca api yaḥ tu bhāvayate sadā iti śrī śivapu0 dharmasaṃhitāyām ṣaḍūiṃśaḥ a dhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca pūrva uktam te dinā ekena pūjitaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ gurūṇām na bhavet kuca vacanam mukha niḥsṛtam viphalam vada tasmāt tvam īśvarāt vadatām vara nāsatya m etat uktam me śṭaṇu vākyam mahā mune krīḍā dine caturdaśyām vṛthā śramaḥ hi bahubhiḥ kleśaiḥ na eva aśnute phalam lokānām hita kāmena kṛtam yena iha tat vada sanatkumāraḥ uvāca āsīt pūrva yuge rājā jaṃbūddīpe su dhārmikaḥ śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca ādhipatyam cakāra saḥ śreṣṭhaḥ veda śāstra athaṃpāragaḥ dadāti anudinam vyāsa teṣām artha striyā ādikam evam rājyam śurutvā dīrgha kālam mahī patiḥ śatānīkaḥ tatas nāmnā sahasrānīkam eva ca sutam jajñe tatas kālāt sitīśaḥ saumṭataḥ tu saḥ kulakam āgatam rājyam ca kresau nṛpa sattamaḥ nyāyataḥ dharmataḥ ca eva rājye śāsti vasuṃdharām kāṃtyā caṃdramasaḥ ca eva pratāpa āditya saṃnibhaḥ truṣu evam sadāpātiḥ pṛthivīṃnyāyatopisaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dadāti īśaḥ yathā tasya pitā anasaḥ atha dīrgheṇa kālena brāhma ṇa asteyata vratāḥ tān āgatān sa saṃprekṣya pūjām cakre yathāvidhi pūjitāḥ te su saṃdṛṣṭāḥ procuḥ nṛpati sattamam dvijāḥ ūcuḥ śṛṇu rājan pravakṣyāmi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ pitrā ate pūjita anityam dāna ācchādana bhojanaiḥ ye kecid brāhmaṇāḥ saṃti yathākāmam yathāsukham saṃvardhitāḥ svaka idha agni sama buddhiḥ ayam nṛpaḥ sāṃpratam tava rājye tu saṃprekṣya ca gatāḥ dvijāḥ vasā meotra parikhinnān nṛpate sa kuṭuṃbinaḥ itas kim kurma evam hiyāsyāmaḥ kutrapīḍitāḥ daridreṇa eva naḥ buddhiḥ yathā śṭaṇu nṛpa uttama paratra nyāyataḥ viprāḥ kiṃcid vakṣyāmi kāraṇam dānāt svargam avāpnoti iha āyātaḥ sukhībhavet samuttasthuḥ samājñāpya rāja ānaṃdīna mānasāḥ samavāyīkṛtāḥ ste tu tathā anyonyam abhāṣata rājā apaṃcatvam āpannaḥ kva asau tiṣṭhati dhārmikaḥ vayam katham na jānīmaḥ saṃśayam paramam gatāḥ gatāni juvha tām vyāsa raviḥ vyākula tām gataḥ rājñām dharmavatām ca api prajāḥ pālayatām sa tām subhikṣam kṣemam eva hi ādityāt jāḥ yateḥ dṛṣṭiḥ vaṣṭeḥ an na samudbhavaḥ annāt saṃjāyate sarvam jagat tṛptiḥ tu sarvadā evam saṃcitya bhagavān ājagāma tatas uraviḥ hi tāyateṣām saṃdeṣṭum dvijaḥ bhūtvā atutān travīt kiṃviṣaṇṇāḥ dvijāyūyam iha īpsataḥ sva karma tat bahūni śubhatī rthāni phala dāni iha sarvatas phalam dātum sva karma phala hātinaḥ pañcayajña phalam nityam catur āśrama vāsinām nityakārī tu naimittā labhet puṇyam śata uttaram sahasra guṇitam kāmyāt tathā āpnoti pumān sadā yaḥ tam mṛtam samākhyāsye t tad purāt āgata ud nṛpam tatas tena veṣayāmāsuḥ harṣāt tvā caturdiśam pattaneṣu pureṣu ca gatvā apaśyan tapasyatam bhārgavam dvijasattamam ūrdhvabāhum nirālaṃbam pādena ekena saṃsthitam tam dṛṣṭa a praṇipatya āśu parivārya dvijottamam japyam tyaktvā su saṃtarpya devān pitṛ gaṇān tathā upaviṣṭān samadrākṣīt kṛtāṃjaliḥ sa pūrvavat pūjayāmāsata ān sarvān pādya ādyaiḥ vidhi pūrvakam paryapṛcchayathānyāyam phala mūlaiḥ su tarpitān tatas te sarvam ācakhyuḥ rājñaḥ durvṛttam ātmanaḥ tathā dṛṣṭasya viprasya yat vākyam tat niśamyasaḥ manasā ciṃtayāmāsa kim kṛtam sukṛtam bhavet tyajet ahaṃtapaḥ kim vā api athavā ārti vināśayet prāṇinām bhaya bhītānām abhayam yat pradīyate aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi yojanāḥ na āṃ pramāṇataḥ yama mārgasya ca adhvānam ācakrāma divākaraḥ na jalam na catatra annam vṛkṣa chāyā sukham nahi śītam vāta aṃdhakāram tu duḥsaha deva dānavaiḥ aṣṭāviṃśati koṭyaḥ tu madhye tāsām yayau raviḥ paśyan sa brāhmaṇaḥ tāṃtu yātanām pāpa karmiṇām ekaikam nirayam tadvat śrūyate kaṃdatām ravaḥ vittaḥ brāhmaṇa ekena tadā alakuṭa pāṇinā bho bho dvija kkaya asyayya amada tvā mama dakṣiṇām yā adattā tepurām atyam kasmin kāle tu tām smara iti uktaḥ sa tutām smṛtvā pratyuvāca dvijaṃprati uktam mayā purāṇa ekam tubhyam tena asmi yācitaḥ gṛham gatvā pradāsyāmi tirobhava mama agratas tam āha asau dvijaḥ teḥ ti su kṛtam ya tḷtam tvayā tvā asau nyāyataḥ saṃpradāpayan gacchamānam tu tam bhūyas gopālaḥ tam tathā adharat kā kiṇi arthe tu gauḥ tasya rakṣitā an atu yācitaḥ ṣaṣ vāc aṃtena dharmasya gṛhītam tasya vai balāt nistejāḥ aśvā bhavat tasmāt gatum ca agrena śaktavān tatas divākaraḥ taṃtu saṃgṛtya āśu kareṇa vai tam dṛṣṭvā pacyamānam tu kuṃbha madhya gatam nṛpam kiṃcid mātra samāśvasya śatānīkam uvāca bho bho rājan pradattāni mahā dānāni ṣoḍaśa brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tvayā apūrva ratnam vastrāṇi ca eva hi grāmān va vividhān ca eva nagarāṇi purāṇi ca kasya idam karmaṇaḥ pāpam yat tvam saṃdatya se sadā tat śrutvā prāhatam rājā aśṛṇu viprayathātatham rājā uvāca mayā adānāni dattāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ yatas tatas su bahūni prajā pīḍana saṃtāpāt samudbhūtaḥ hutāśanaḥ tena datyāmi aham viprāḥ preta saṃsthā divāniśam sutasya mā iyat īhā asti muktiḥ pāpāt su duḥsahāt etat śrutvā vacaḥ rājñaḥ sa vipra śva ātma kāraṇāt mānuṣāṇām hita arthāya paryapṛcchat divākaram vipraḥ uvāca sādhūnām darśanam puṇya tīrtha bhūta ahi sādhavaḥ kālena phalate tīrtha sadyas sādhu samāgamaḥ na ca eva akṛta puṇyānām deve bhaktiḥsu jāyate vipreṣu ca viśeṣeṇa tathā sādhu tapasviṣu yadā a pāpa kṣayaḥ puṃsām dānedhyān etadā matiḥ tasmāt eva param devam manye ham tvām na saṃśayaḥ yenapā mānavaḥ saṃsāre patitaḥ lokaḥ kṣetra dāra gṛha ādiṣu kim na prāpnoti saṃmūḍhaḥ svarga mokṣa sukhāni ca śṛṇu vipra yathātathyam lokānām hita kāmyayā pṛṣṭaḥ tehaṃkṛtaḥ te yaḥ dharmaḥ saṃvardhayiṣyati tatas śuddhā sujivhāyāḥ tasmāt āpnoti asaṃśayaḥ devatānām priyam tatra svargāt āryāḥ āṃti sarvadā krīḍā artha bhuktim ādāya saṃvi hṛtya punar punar su saṃtuṣṭāḥ bāla rūpam sa mā āsthāya sukanyā rūpibhiḥ gaṇaiḥ śivāya ca anya devebhyaḥ prekṣaṇam ca mahā utsavam teṣām dhāma tuyānti ete ye bhavaṃti ati pāpinaḥ tasmāt caturdaśīm ṛ uṣṇām śuklām vā samupoṣya ca ekadiva dadyāt dhenum dvijātibhyaḥ śivāya parikalpitām evam hatvā ca pāpāni yāti svargam na saṃśayaḥ etat śrutvā āsa sūryeṇa saha amātya dvijottamān tatas sa rājā atu su saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ śrutvā vacaḥ tasya dvijottamasya saraḥ sa dṛṣṭvā eva nikhanyamānam pṛṣṭvā tu mūlyena cakāra karma dine dine yāvat abhūt suvarṇa tathā ca go mūlyam aśeṣa dānam tatas pradṛṣṭaḥ prayayau sva deśam su rakṣitam maṃtri varaiḥ tathā nṛpaiḥ dvijopadi ṭaṃma cakāra rājā vratam yathāvat ca tat eva dānam ārutya yānam su vimānam agryam saṃkrīḍamānaḥ sahasā apsarobhiḥ idam vataṃyaḥ kurute su samyak aikānhikam vyāsa śiva prasādāt labhet divam pūrva pitāmahaiḥ saha nihatya pāpāni purā kṛtāni samupoṣya yatnāt saṃpūjya dhenum pradyāt dijasattama āyatasya a abhāvāt su ghṛtasya pātram sa vyaṃjanam vastra yutam saha annam yat labhate sudhenāḥ nihatya pāpāni purā kṛtāni divam prayāti iha na saṃśayaḥ tra ciram ti uṣitvā āsatuḥ rudra loka rājā abhavet atra su dharma śīlaḥ ekām prakuryāt su śubhām vai saṃte caturdaśīm satya yutaḥ samam hi tuṣṭiḥ yathā syāt iha śaṃkarasya maṃtreṇa valāt śopi maṃtra ātmakāḥ sarva aimehi devāḥ su yakṣa rakṣaḥ pitaraḥ manuṣyāḥ maṃtrāṇi ca uktāni te smin taiḥ arcanīyaḥ bhagavān pinākī kurvan su kṛcchra hi catur dināni caturdaśī vyāsa upoṣaṇīyā ekādaśyām eka bhaktam sakṛt pānīya me vaca a yācitaṃtu dvādaśyām sa naktāca trayodaśī caturdaśī nirāhārā kartavyā a ca mahāvrate pauṇimāyām tu godānam phalam ka tvā tat anute ātmanaḥ kiṃcid bhāva udayāt dijātaye śivaḥ saṃprīyatām evam iti uktvā phalam aśnute vratasya asya sa magrasya dravya abhāvāt śṛṇuṣva tat palaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ pātram śulvasya tu tad ardhakam ghṛtena hiraṇyam tukārayet vastreṇa veṣṭayitvā tu tad abhāvāt sa sūtrakam dadyāt tat dijamukhyāya śivaḥ saṃprīyatā m iti sthāṇum īśam jagannātham śūlapāṇi maheśvaram praṇataḥ asmi bhūtanātham same pāpam vyapohatu kapāla mālinam praṇataḥ asmi jagannātham sam me pāpam vyapohatu caṃdra ardha dhāriṇam devam sarva ābharaṇa bhūpitam triśūla pāṇi naṃtrya kṣatripatha aṃka su dhāriṇam yaḥ śva ahaṃkāra kaḥ rudraḥ same pāpam vyapohatu evam pūjya śivam maṃtraiḥ statas dānam prakalpayet surūpāḥ subhagāḥ te tu jāyate bhokriṇaḥ dhanam evam yaḥ kurute samyak caturmāsyāḥ caturdaśīm dvayam yathā śatānīkaḥ yāti asau śāṃkaram padam kulānām śatam uddhṛtya nippāpī surapū jitaḥ yat niśāyām tathā prātar yat madhya anha aparāhnayoḥ saṃdhyāyām cakṛtam pāpam karmaṇā a manasā a girā iti śrī śiva saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ aṣṭāviṃśe mahā puṇyam śiva nāma sahasrakam tat sarvam nāśam āyāti toya stham lavaṇam yathā evam vā kurute yaḥ tu cāturmāsī vidhānataḥ evam yaḥ pūjayet bhaktyā caturdaśyām tu śaṃkaram sahasam kīrtayet nāmnām śṭaṇuyāt vā api bhaktitaḥ niyama stthaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca kathayasva samāsena lokānām hita kāmyayā śiva nāmnām sahasram tu iha amutra phala pradam mune śṭaṇu pravakṣyāmi sarva agha ogha vināśanam prakhyātum nā api śaktaḥ aham prasādāt ca eva tasya hi prāpya anujñām tatas stotram dhyānam āgāt tat aiśvaram yadā tena abhyanujñātaḥ na iva tadā abhavam nāmnām kiṃcid samuddeśam vadaye ca avyakta yoninaḥ śṛṇu nāma sahasram tu yat uktam padmayoninā daśa nāma sahasrāṇām sahasram tu pitāmahaḥ gireḥ sāram yathā hema tathā etat sāram uddhṛtam śāṃtikam pauṣṭikam ca eva rakṣaḥ ghnam pāvanam mahat idam bhaktāya dātavyam śraddadhāna āstikāya ca an āśraddadhāna rūpāya anāstikāya jita ātmane yaḥ ca abhyasūyate devaṃbhūta ātmānam pinākinam sa kṛṣṇa narakaṃyāti saha pūrvaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ idam jñātvā aṃta kāle pi sa gacchet paramām gatim pavitram maṃgalam puṇyam kalyāṇam idam utamam nigadiṣye iti aham vyāsa stavānām uttamam stavam idam bahmā purā kṛtvā sarva loka pitāmahaḥ sarva stavānām divyānām rāja tve samakalpayat tadā prabhṛti ca eva ayam īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ tadā prabhṛti ca eva ayam parāṇām api yaḥ paraḥ śāṃtānām apiyā śāṃtiḥ yutīnām apiyā dyutiḥ yoginām api yaḥ yogī kāraṇānām ca kāraṇam yatas lokāḥ saṃbhavaṃti na bhavanti yatas punar aṣṭottarasahasram tu nāmnām īśasya meś śṛṇu yat śrutvā tvam muni śreṣṭha sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi om sthiraḥ sthāṇuḥ prabhuḥ bhānuḥ pravaraḥ vara daḥ varaḥ jaṭī vama śikhī khagī sarva aṃgaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ haraḥ ca hariṇa akṣa śva sarva bhūta haraḥ prabhuḥ śmaśānacārī bhagavān khecara ukhacara udbhavaḥ abhivaṃdyaḥ mahā karmā tapasvī bhūta bhāvanaḥ mahī rūpaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sarva rūpaḥ mahā aśanaḥ viśvarūpaḥ u virūpaśva viśvabhuj vāmanaḥ manuḥ lokapāla aṃtarhita ātmā prasādā uha ya gardabhī pavitra śva mahān ca eva niyamaḥ niyama āśrayaḥ sarva varmā asvayaṃbhūḥ ca anādiḥ ādiḥ avyayaḥ saumya rūpaḥ virūpā kṣaḥ somaḥ nakṣatra sādhakaḥ caṃdraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ ketuḥ grahaḥ graha patiḥ varaḥ adriḥ adri ālayaḥ kartā amṭaga bāṇa arpaṇa unaghaḥ saṃvatsara karaḥ maṃtraḥ pramāṇam paramam tapaḥ mahāmātraḥ mahā tapāḥ suvarṇaretāḥ sarvajñaḥ subījaḥ vṛṣavāhanaḥ daśabāhuḥ tu animiṣaḥ nīlakaṃṭha aumāpatiḥ viśvarūpaḥ svayam śreṣṭhaḥ uba liḥ vairocanoḥ iha ā gaṇakartā gaṇapatiḥ digvāsāḥ kāmyaḥ eva ca kamaṃḍalu dharaḥ dhanvī bāṇa hastaḥ pratāpavān aśaniḥ śataghnī khagī paṭṭiśī cāyudhī mahān uṣṇīṣī ca suvakraḥ ca atyugraḥ vinataḥ tathā dīrghaśva harinetra śva satīrthaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca śṭagāla rūpaḥ sarva arthaḥ muṃḍaḥ kuṃḍī kamaṃḍaluḥ ajaḥ ca mṛgarūpa śvagaṃdhama alīka parddhapi ūrdhvaretāḥ ūrdhvaliṃgaḥ ūrdhvaśāyī nabhastalaḥ trija ṭīcīravāsāḥ ca rudraḥ senāpatiḥ vibhuḥ siṃha śārdūla rūpaḥ ca ārdra śvarma adhara adharaḥ sarvāḥ vāsaḥ catuṣpathaḥ nṛtyapriyaḥ nṛtya tṛpmonartakaḥ savilāsakaḥ poṣaḥ mahā tapāḥ prāṃśuḥ nityaḥ giri caraḥ nabhaḥ dakṣa yajña apahārīca supathaḥ madhyamaḥ tathā gaṃbhīra ghoṣaḥ gaṃbhīraḥ gaṃbhīra bala vāhanaḥ kṣṇa daśanaḥ ca eva mahākāyaḥ mahā ānanaḥ viṣvaksenaḥ hariḥ yajñaḥ saṃyuga āpīḍa vāhanaḥ tīkṣṇa bāhu śva hari akṣaḥ mahāyaḥ karma kāla vid viṣṇu prasāditaḥ yajñaḥ samudraḥ vaḍavāmukhaḥ laṃbana ulaṃbita uṣṭha śva bahu māyā payonidhiḥ mahā aṃga śva mahā daṃṣṭraḥ mahā jivhaḥ mahā makhaḥ mahānakhaḥ mahāromā mahākeśaḥ mahājaṭaḥ vṛkṣakāraḥ yakṣaketuḥ taralaḥ vāyuvāhanaḥ maṃḍalī vāyudhām ācade vadānava darpa hā prakāśaḥ jaṃgamaḥ tathā amogha artha prasāda śva a bhigamyaḥ sudarśanaḥ upahāraḥ priyaḥ sarvaḥ kanakaḥ kāṃcana sthiraḥ tapanaḥ tāpana śvādyaḥ ghṛṇīyajñaḥ samāhitaḥ mugaṇaḥ gaṇa kāraḥ ca bhūtabhāvana sārathiḥ bhasmaśāyī bhasma rūkṣaḥ bhasmarūpaḥ taraṃgaṇaḥ a gaṇaḥ ca eva lopaḥ ca mahātmā sarva pūjitaḥ śaṃkuḥ triśaṃku saṃpannaḥ śuciḥ bhūta niṣevitaḥ śākhaḥ viśākhaḥ kuṃbhāṃḍa śvārthajālaḥ su niśvayaḥ kapilaḥ śūra āyuḥ ca eva apara uragaḥ avijñeyaḥ susārathiḥ paraśvadha āyudhaḥ devaḥ artha kāraḥ sudhīḥ varaḥ tuṃbavīṇaḥ mahākopaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ jaleśayaḥ ugra vaṃśa karaḥ vaṃśa vaṃśa dhārā uti aniṃditaḥ sarva aṃga rūpaḥ māyāvī bāṃdhavaḥ baṃdhukartā acasubaṃdhuḥ avilocanaḥ kuru vāsī suyajñāriḥ mukāmāriḥ mahādaṃṣṭraḥ samaḥ yudhi bāhuḥ tu aniṃditaḥ sarvaḥ śaṃkara odhana dodhanaḥ amara īśaḥ mahādevaḥ viśvadevaḥ su rāri hā dīdhitiśva ahiḥ budhyaśva cekitānaḥ hariḥ tathā dhanvaṃtariḥ dhūmake tuḥskaṃdaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ tathā dhātā śakraḥ ca viṣṇu śva mitraḥ tvaṣṭā adhruvaḥ dhanaḥ prabhāvaḥ sarva go vāyuḥ aryamā savitā araviḥ udagra śva vidhātā acamāṃdhātā abhūtabhāvanaḥ guṇa āvahaḥ balavān śva upaśāṃta śva purāṇaḥ puṇya caṃcurī kuruḥ vai dṛṣṭvā rāmaḥ abhyayāt vanāt bāhūnām tasya bhārgavaḥ jagāma tapase dhīmān maheṃdra adrau saṃvīryavān jagāma atha śramam kartum sarāmaḥ hara sannidhau arjunasya sutāḥ te tu saṃbhūya ayodhayan tatas asatu mahā tejāḥ kṛtvā ācā akṣatriyām dharām tatas kṣatriya vīrāṇām yoṣitaḥ vanam āśrayan putrān tu lebhire tatas tat utthitam dṛṣṭvā punar kṣatram sa bhārgavaḥ punar śata sahasrāṇi hatvā rājñām mahā yaśāḥ cakāra bhārgavaḥ sarvām mahīm śoṇita kardamām tatas da tvā dvijebhyaḥ tām mahīm sarvām sa bhārgavaḥ punar te kṣatriyā vyāsa trāhmaṇebhyaḥ prajajñire te ca vṛddha amahā vīryāḥ pṛthivīpatayaḥ kārya yadi icchet śreyaḥ ātmanaḥ vacasā a manasā avāpi karmaṇā api ihaya tsamam kṛtvā apāpāni aśeṣāṇi tulādānam karoti yaḥ pāpa kṛtam yat divase niśāyām dvis saṃdhyayoḥ madhyadine niśāṃtayoḥ bālena adhyāyaiḥ kīrtyate sa udbhava kṣayam dadāti evam tu yaḥ vyāsa tulāpuruṣam uttamam hatvā pāpam divam tiṣṭhet yāvat iṃdrāḥ caturdaśa iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām tulāpuruṣavarṇanam nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca dānānām tat mama ākhyāhi mānuṣāṇām hita arthataḥ śṛṇu kāleya yad dānāt phala viṃdati mānavaḥ ekasmāt api sarveṣām dānānām tat śṛṇuṣva me dānānām uttamam dānam brahmāṃḍam khalu mānavaiḥ dātavyam mukti kāmaiḥ tu saṃsāra uttāraṇāya vai sarveṣu eva manonugaiḥ sa bahubhiḥ brahmāṃḍadaḥ krīḍate paścāt yāti param su durlabha padam devaiḥ mune mādhavaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan brūhi brahmāṃḍam yat pramāṇam yad ātmakam yad ādhāram yathā jātam yena me pratyayaḥ bhavet muneḥ ṭaṇu pravakṣyāmi yat utsedham tu vistaram brahmāṃḍaṃtu su saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu pāpāt pramucyate yat tat kāraṇam avyaktam śivam padmanāmayam tasmāt saṃjāyate vyoma puṣkarāt vāyu saṃbhavaḥ tasmāt saṃjāyate brahmā dvīdhā bhūtāt vikālataḥ tasya ādhāraḥ sitaḥ nāgaḥ saca viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ śeṣa ākhyāya guṇān vaktum na śaktāḥ deva dānavāḥ siddhaiḥ deva ṛṣi gaṇa pūjitaḥ phaṇāmaṇi sahasreṇa svasti kāmala bhūṣaṇaḥ mada āghūrṇita netra usausa agniḥ śvetā eva acalaḥ sadā eva eka kuṃḍalaḥ sāyaṃgaṃgā pravāheṇa śveta hāra upaśobhitaḥ nīla vāsāma da udriktaḥ kailāsa adriḥ iva unnataḥ lāṃgala āsakta hasta agraḥ viśvat musalam uttamam upāsyate svayam kanyayā avāruṇyena mūrtayā saṃkarṣaṇa ātmakaḥ rudraḥ viṣa anala śikhā jvalaḥ āste kṣiti maṃḍalam viśva tsarṣapa vat bhūtam śeṣa uśeṣa sura arcitaḥ tasya vīryam prabhāvaḥ ca śakyam vā a tridaśaiḥ api na hi varṇayitum jñātum sva rūpam rūpam eva ca āste kusuma mālā iva phaṇāmaṇi śilā aruṇā yasya epā sakalā pṛthvī kaḥ tat vīrya vadiṣyati yadā avijṛṃbhata enam tomada āghūrṇita locanaḥ tadā acala tibhūḥ eṣā asa adri toya abdhi kānanā na antam guṇānām gacchaṃti siddhā muni su kinnarāḥ gaṃdharva uraga deva aśvatena anaṃtaḥ yam avyayaḥ muhur śvāsa anila apāḥ taṃ lohitam haricaṃdanam yasya nāga vadhū hastaiḥ diśām yāti su vāsatām jñātavān sakalam ca eva gaga jyotīṃṣita tvataḥ yama arāḥ dhyā purāṇa ṛṣiḥ nimitta paṭhitam phalam bibharti mālām lokānām śirasā vivṛtā mahī tena iyam nāga vīryeṇa sa deva asura mānuṣā n mahat ca sutalam ca agryam ucchrāyam dviguṇam ca eṣām sarveṣām ratna bhūmayaḥ ratna vam toya prāsāda abhūmayaḥ hema saṃbhavāḥ teṣu dānava daiteyānām gānām jātayaḥ tathā nivasaṃti mahābhāga arākṣasāḥ daitya saṃbhavāḥ prāha svargasadām madhye pātālāni iti nāradaḥ nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣā sumaṇayaḥ yatra su prabhāḥ āhlāda kāriṇaḥ śubhrāḥ mā āleka syana prīti rita śveta śva śobhate bhakṣya bhojya anna pānāni bhujyaṃte muditaiḥ bha śam puṃskokila rutaṃtatra vanyāni kamala ākarāḥ nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ramyāḥ ṇi manojñāni aṃbarāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ati śuśvāṇi gaṃdha āḍhyam ca anulepanam vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṃgānām kha nāgeyāni ca dvija tapasā a samavāpta anidānavaiḥ siddha mānavaiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām brahmāṃḍakathanaṃnāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ teṣām ūrdhva upariṣṭāt vainara kāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva me vadataḥ me muni śreṣṭha pacyaṃte yatra pāpinaḥ vaitaraṇī pūyavahā ka milaḥ kṛmibhojanaḥ a sipatravanam tathā apūya vaha apāyaḥ bahi valaḥ vyadhaḥ śirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kālasūtraḥ catamaśva avīci rodhanaḥ śvabhojanā upyadṛṣṭaśva mahārauravaśālmalī pacyaṃte te iṣu puruṣāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ tuye na avi praṃsuḥ āsavam bhrūṇa hā apara sva hartā gorodhaḥ viśva ghātakaḥ taiḥ guroḥ vā sādhvī vikraya rudh vāla vadhakī keśa vikrayī avamantā a gurūṇām yaḥ paśu addhā uktā anara adhamaḥ agamya gāmīya śva api yāti tata khalam dvija avīci rodhe patati maryādādūṣa kaḥ tathā deva dvija pitṛ ddeṣṭa arana dūṣayitā cayaḥ śastra kūṭa kṛt naraḥ a yājya yājakaḥ ca eva tathā eva abhakṣya bhakṣakaḥ mitra hā madhu hāya ati krūrām vaitaraṇīm nadīm teḥ uṣṇeyāṃtya śauca aśva kuhaka ājīvinaḥ caye pāti aṃte dvija tatraivayaḥ ca apāpa iṣu vanhi daḥ vratasya lopa koyaśva sva āśramāt vicyuta āśvaye sam daṃśeyātanā madhye pataṃti bhṛśa dāruṇe divāsvapneṣu skaṃdaṃti yena rātrahmacāriṇaḥ ete ca anye ca narakāḥ śataśas utha sahasraśas yeṣu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ pacyate yātanām gatāḥ tathā eva pāpāni etāni tathā anyāni saha sraśas bhujyaṃteya ani puruṣaiḥ nara kāṃtara gocaraiḥ varṇa āśrama viruddham ca karma kurvaṃti ye narāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācāni adhas śirobhiḥ dṛśyam tena arakāḥ divi daivataiḥ devān adhomukhān sarvān na ca paśyaṃti nārakāḥ sthāvarāḥ lama yona aśvapakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ umṭagāḥ dhārmikāḥ tridaśāḥ tadvat mokṣiṇaḥ śva yathākramam yāvaṃtaḥ jaṃtavaḥ svarge tāvantaḥ nara kaukasaḥ pāpaḥ udyāti narakam prāyaścitta parāṅmukhaḥ pāpānām anurūpāṇi prāyaścittāni ya yathā prāyaścittāni kāleya manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ bravīt yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇām tāni karmāṇi aghāni vai prāyaścittam aśeṣāṇām hara anusmaraṇam param prāyaścittam tu tasya ekam yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate param maheśvaram avāpnoti madhyān hāḥ diṣu saṃsmaran prātar niśi ca saṃdhyāyām sadyas pāpa kṣayam naraḥ muktim prayāti svarga āptiḥ samasta kleśa saṃkṣayaḥ tasya aṃtarā ayaḥ vipra iṃdra japa homa arcana ādiṣu śivam aharniśam tasmāt saṃkṣīṇa aśeṣa pātake tat eva prītaye bhūtvā punar duḥkhāya jāyate tasmāt duḥkha ātmakam kiṃcid sukha ātmakam manasaḥ pariṇāmaḥ yaḥ sukha duḥkha upalakṣaṇam jñānam eva param brahma jñānam tad tvāya kalpate jñāna ātmakam idam vi śñjñānāt na vidyate param evam etat mayā ākhyātam sarva naraka maṃḍalam maṃḍalam bhuvaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pārāśarya su saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu tvaṃvada tomama śālmali śva kuśaḥ śva puṣkaraḥ śākaḥ tu samamaḥ sarve samudraiḥ samabhiḥ ṭatāḥ jaṃbūdvīpaḥ samastānām eteṣām madhyamaḥ sthitaḥ pra viṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt yojanaiḥ tasya ca ucchrayaḥ caturaśīti sāhasraiḥ dvātriṃśat mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ mūleḥ ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ himavān hemakūṭa śva niṣadha śvā sya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṃgī ca auttarevarṣaparvatāḥ daśa sāhastrika atyete ratnavaṃtā uruṇa prabhāḥ bhāratam prathamam varṣam tatas kiṃpuruṣam smṛtam ilāvatam ṛṣi śreṣṭha catvāraḥ cātra parvatāḥ viṣkam bhāracitā meroḥ yojana ayutam ucchritāḥ pūrveṇa maṃdaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gaṃdhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime bhāge supārśva śrū uttare sthitaḥ kadaṃbaḥ jaṃbū vṛkṣa śvapippala uvaṭaḥ eva ca ekādaśa śata āyāmāḥ pādapā giri ketavaḥ jaṃbūdvīpasya ayaḥ jaṃvūḥ nāma hetuḥ mahā mune mahāgaja pramāṇāni jaṃboḥ tasya phalāni ca patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvatas rasena teṣām vi khyātā tatra jaṃbūnadī iti vai tat pāna svastha manasām janānām tatra jāyate tīremṭat tatra saṃprāpya sukha vāyu viśoṣitā jāṃbūnada ākhyam bhavati suvarṇa siddha bhūṣaṇa m bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālam ca paścime varṣet detu muni śreṣṭha tayoḥ madhya elā vṛtam vanam caitraratham pūrve dakṣiṇe gaṃdhamādanam viśvājam paścime tadvat uttarenaṃdanam smṛtam aruṇodam mahābhadram śītodam mānasam smṛtam sarāṃsi etāni ca tu āri deva bhogyāni sarvaśas sītāṃjanaḥ kumudaśva kuraraḥ mālyavān tathā ve kaṃka pramukhāḥ meroḥ pūrvatas kesara acalāḥ su nīla niṣadha atrikūṭaḥ śiśiraḥ ca eva patagaḥ rajataḥ tathā niṣadha ādayaḥ dakṣiṇatas tasya kesara parvatāḥ kapilaḥ gaṃdhamādanaḥ jārudhi pramukhāḥ tadvat paścimekesara acalāḥ mahīdharaḥ tathā uttare kesara acalāḥ caturdaśa sahasrāṇi brahmaṇaḥ prathitam divi iṃdra ādi lokapālānām diśāsu vidiśāsu ca tasya samaṃtataḥ ca aṣṭau khyātāḥ puryaḥ samaṃtataḥ samaṃtāt brahmaṇaḥ puryāḥ plāvayi tvā iṃdu maṃḍalam sītā ca alakanaṃdā ca caturdhā pratipadyate sītā pūrveṇa śailāt tu naṃdā ca eva tu dakṣiṇe kalān kalān catur diś su mahā aṃbudhim sā āyayau prayatā bhūtvā gaṃgā tripathagāminī gaṃdhamādanau teṣām madhya gataḥ meruḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ bharatāḥ ketumāla aśva bhadrāśvāḥ kuravaḥ tathā maryādā āloka bātyataḥ jaṭharet eva kūṭaḥ ca āyāmet dakṣiṇa uttare dakṣiṇa uttaram āyātau kaṇikā aṃtar vyavasthitau jaṭharāyāḥ sthita ameroḥ yeṣām ddau dvau vyavasthitau kesarāḥ parvatāḥ eva īśīta āḍhyāḥ su manoramāḥ śailānām aṃtare droṇyaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ su ramyāṇi su ramyāṇi sarveṣām ca eva devānām yakṣa gaṃdharva rakṣasām krīḍanti deva daiteyāḥ śaila droṇīṣu aharniśam dharmiṇām ālaya atyeta bhaumāḥ svargāḥ prakīrtitāḥ na eteṣu pāpa kartāraḥ yānti paśyaṃti kutracid yāni kiṃpuruṣāyāni varṣāṇi aṣṭau mahā mune na tepu śoka una āyāsa una uddegaḥ kṣudh bhaya ādikam svasthāḥ prajā nirātaṃkāḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ daśa dvādaśa varṣāṇām sahasrāṇi sthira āyuṣaḥ kṛta tretā ādikāḥ ca eva bhaumāni aṃbhāṃsi sarvatas kalpanā saptasu eta iṣu nadī aśva su payāḥ svarṇavālu kāḥ śataśas saṃti kṣudra aśvatāṃsu krīḍā subhājanāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām bahmāṃḍa kathanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vakṣye iham himādreḥ ca eva dakṣiṇam uttaram tu samudrasya bhāratī yatra saṃsṛtiḥ nāgaddīpaḥ tathā asaumyaḥ gāṃdharvaḥ tu athavā aruṇaḥ ayam tu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahasram tu dvīpaḥ yam dakṣiṇa uttaraḥ pūrve kirātāḥ ayasyasyuḥ paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ āṃdhrā dakṣiṇatas vyāsa turuṣkāḥ stu api ca uttare brāhmaṇāḥ sa triyā vaiśyā madhyeśūdrāḥ ca bhāgaśas maheṃdraḥ malayaḥ sadyas śuktimātṛ kṣaparva taḥ kulaparvatāḥ vedasmṛti mukhā nadyaḥ pāriyātra udbhavā mune narmadā surasā ādya āśva saṃtya nyāśva sahasraśas viṃdhyodbhavā mahānadyaḥ sarva pāpa harāḥ śubhāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī tāpī pramukha toyagāḥ viṃdhyāḥ dvi nirgatāḥ puṇyāḥ snānāt pāpa bhaya apahāḥ satyapāda udbhavā nadyaḥ kṛṣṇaveṇī ādikāḥ tathā kṛtamālā tākhaparṇī pramukhāḥ malaya udbhavāḥ triyāmā ṛṣikulyā ādyā maheṃdra prabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ṛṣikulyāḥ kumāryāyāḥ śuktima tvāt asaṃbhavāḥ nā nā janapadāḥ teṣuvai saṃtomaṃḍaleṣuvai āsā anusaṃti ruta ādīni na ca anyeṣu ddīpeṣu prabha ca atra yajvanaḥ yatas hi karma bhūḥ eṣā jaṃbūddīpe mahā mune tatra api bhāratam śreṣṭham atas nyābhogabhūmayaḥ atra janma sahasrāṇām mānuṣyam puṇya saṃcayam gāyaṃti devāḥ kila gītakāni bhavaṃti bhūyas puruṣāḥ sura tvāt avāpya mānuṣya mayam kadācid vihṛtya śaṃbhau parama ātma bhūte prāpsyati dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyāḥ avayam kṛtāḥ karmaṇi saṃniviṣṭāḥ sukhāyate lakṣa yojana vistāram jaṃbūdvīpam jaya ākhyātam kṣāra udadhi su saṃvṛtam saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhim śata sāhasra saṃmitam somakaḥ sumanāḥ śailā vaiśyājaḥ ca eva saptamaḥ varṣa acala iṣu ramya iṣu muditāḥ satatam prajāḥ vasaṃti deva gaṃdharvā varṣeṣu eteṣu nityaśas na ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ vā api janānām tam tra kutracid daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvaṃti māna vāḥ anutamā śikhā caiva pāpaghnī tridivā rūpā sanā eva anyatra nimnagāḥ kṣudranayaḥ tathā śai lāḥ tathā saṃti sahasraśas tāḥ pibaṃti su saṃdṛṣṭāḥ nadīḥ janapadāḥ tu te na tatrāsti yuga avasthā yathā sthāneṣu saptasu nisattama prāvṛkṣa pramāṇaḥ tu tad madhye su mahā taruḥ ijyate tatra bhaga vān śaṃkaraḥ loka śaṃkaraḥ saṃkṣepeṇa tathā bhūyas śālmali tvam niśāmaya sama varṣāṇi tatra eva teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu śālmalena tu vṛkṣeṇa tena śālmali saṃjñitaḥ dviguṇena samudreṇa satatam saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ varṣa āśi vyaṃjikān agre tāsām nāmāni imā śṛṇu śukla a raktā nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsām puṇya toyāḥ su śāṃti dāḥ sanā etāni tu varṣāṇi catur varṇa yutāni tu eṣa dvīpaḥ samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ dviguṇenakuśa dvīpaḥ samaṃtāt vā ati atas sthitaḥ vasaṃti tatra daiteyām anujaiḥ saha dānavāḥ tathā eva deva gaṃdharva yakṣāḥ kiṃpuruṣa ādayaḥ varṇāḥ tatra eva catvāraḥ nija anuṣṭhāna tatparāḥ kuśeśayaḥ hariḥ ca eva dyutimān puṣpavān tathā maṇidrumaḥ mahāśailaḥ samamaḥ maṃdara acalaḥ nadī aśva saptatāsām tu nāmā niśṛṇuta tvataḥ dhūta pāpa aśiva acaiva pavitra asaṃmi tiḥ tathā vidyā raṃbhā mahīcānyā sarva pāpa harāḥ tu imāḥ anyāḥ sahasraśas saṃti śubha apaḥ hema vālukāḥ kuśa dvī pekuśaḥ tam krauṃcadvīpaḥ mahābhāga śrūyatāṃcā romahān dviguṇena samudreṇa dadhimaṃḍa uda kāṭataḥ varṣa acalāḥ mahābuddha teṣām nāmāni imā śṛṇu krauṃcaḥ ca eva amanaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ vā aṃdhakārakaḥ manācā eva duṃdubhiḥ nivasaṃtinirātam kāvarṣa śaila iṣu teṣu vai sarva sauvarṇa ramya iṣu sahadeva gaṇaiḥ prajāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdra aśva anukrama uditāḥ saṃti tatra mahā nadyaḥ sapta anyāḥ tu sahasraśas gaurī kumudvatī ca eva saṃdhyā rātriḥ manojavā khyāti śva puṃḍarīka ācayāḥ pibaṃti payaḥ śubham dadhimaṃḍa udaka śvāpi śāka dvīpana saṃsṛtaḥ dviguṇena adrayaḥ sama teṣām nāmāni imā śṛṇu śyāmaḥ yaḥ tam giriḥ ca eva kesarī śākaḥ tatra mahā vṛkṣaḥ siddha gaṃdharva sevitaḥ tatra pu ṇyā janapadāḥ cāturvarṇya samanvitāḥ nadī aśvātra mahā puṇyāḥ sarva pāpa bhaya apahāḥ mukumārī kumārīca nalinī veṇukā āda yā gabhastiḥ mahīdharāḥ tathā asaṃtiśataśas tha sahasraśas dharma hāniḥ nateṣu asti svargāt āgatya mānavāḥ saṃgharṣaḥ parasparam sūryaḥ sadā kṣīrodena āvṛtaḥ saḥ api dviguṇena samaṃtataḥ kṣīrābdhiḥ sarvatas vyāptaḥ puṣkara ākhyeṇa saṃvṛtaḥ dviguṇena mahāvarṣaḥ tatra khyātaḥ utha mānasaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi paṃca ūrdhva samucchri taḥ tāvatā eva tulakṣāṇi sarvatas valaya ākṛtiḥ tena eva valaya ākāra ddaya va rṣa sama ākṛtiḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvaṃti mānavāḥ nirāmaya avīta śoka arāga dveṣa vivarjitāḥ satya anṛtena tasyāḥ tāṃsadā eva vasatiḥ sadā tulya veṣāḥ tu manujāḥ hema varṇa eka rūpiṇaḥ puṣkare dhātakīkhaṃḍe mahāvīta mahāmu ne tasmin nivasate brahmā a pūjyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ svādu udakena aṃbudhinā puṣkaram pariveṣṭitam evaṃddīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ dvīpaḥ ca eva paraiḥ nyūna atirikta tāta iṣām samudra iṣu samā ivai śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ kṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śataśas tat daśa uttaram samudrāṇām muni śreṣṭha sarveṣām kathitam tam vai bhojanam puṣkaradvīpe prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadā eva hi dviguṇa a hiraṇmayī bhūmiḥ jaṃtu vivarjitā lokālokaḥ tatas śailaḥ sahasrāḥ ucchrāyeṇa catāvat hi yojana ayuta vistṛtaḥ tamaḥ cāṃḍa kaṭāhena sā iyam urvī mahā mune paṃcāśat koṭi vi stārā samaddīpā mahīdharā ādhāra bhūtā a sarveṣām sarva bhūta guṇa adhikā sā iyam dhātrī ca kāleya sarveṣām jagatām ilā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām bhuvanakośavarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tāvat pramāṇā pṛthivī bhūḥ lokaḥ satuc īyate yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa eva parisaṃkhyayā paricakṣate raveḥ ūrdhva śaśīta sthaula kṣayaḥ jana saṃkhyayā grahāṇām maṃḍalam kṛttram śaśinā upari saṃsthitam saptarṣi maṃḍalam sma alakṣam ekam tu saṃsthitam ṛṣibhyaḥ tu sahasrāṇām śatāt ūrdhva vyavasthitaḥ dhruvāt ūrdhvam ahar lokaḥ saba ete brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ sanakaśva sanaṃdaśva tṛtīyaśva sanātanaḥ kapilaḥ vāsuriḥ ca eva voḍhaḥ paṃcaśikhaḥ tathā vairāja āyatra vaidevāḥ sthitā dāha vivarjitāḥ nirūpya evam mahī gola sūrya ādi sthiti varṇanam paṃcatriṃśe abhidhāsyate satya dharma ratāḥ ca eva jñāninaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ saṃtihi mānavāḥ bhuvar loke tu va rūpiṇaḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ nāgāḥ sura ādayaḥ nava graha gaṇāḥ statra ṛṣayaḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ pātālāni ca samā eva brahmāṃḍa sya ca vistaraḥ etat aṃḍa kaṭāham ca sarvatas vai samāvṛtam payasā adaśaguṇena sarvatas tat samāvṛtam va dvinā vāyunā ca eva nabhasā tamasā tathā bhūtādinā api mahatā daśa uttareṇa veṣṭitam mahāntam ca samāgatya pradhānapuruṣaḥ sthitaḥ anaṃtasya natasya astisaṃkhyāpi paramātmanaḥ tena anaṃtaḥ eti khyātaḥ pramāṇam na api vaiyataḥ hetu bhūtaḥ samastasya prakṛtiḥ sā aparā mune aṃḍānām tu sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca īdṛśāni prabhūtāni tasmāt avyakta janmanaḥ dārūṇi agniḥ yayā tailam vilaṣu payasi ghṛtam ādi bījāt prabhavanti tatas tebhyaḥ māḥ tebhyaḥ putrāḥ tathā anyeṣām bījāni anya ani vaiyataḥ mahat ādayaḥ viśeṣataḥ tat bhavanti sura ādayaḥ bījāt ṛkṣa prarohe ṇa ya thāna apacayaḥ taroḥ sūryakānta maṇeḥ prajāyate tadvat saṃjāyate sṛṣṭiḥ śivaḥ tatra na kāmayet śiva śakti samāyoge deva ādyāḥ prabhavanti hi brahma a viṣṇu śva rudra śva sa śivaḥ parigīyate kartā akriyāṇām parigīyate munayaḥ ūcuḥ paḍakṣaram tvayā proktam purā sarva artha sādhakam śivasya paramam maṃtram bhukti mukti karam śivam vayam tu śrotum icchāmaḥ maṃtrān parama sādhanān yaiḥ purā munayaḥ siddhāḥ śivāt amara tāṃgatāḥ sūta māṃḍavya ādayaḥ sarva etān sarva astvam vai dasvanaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca pravakṣyāmi tam śaṃbhoḥ yat uktam hi purā kila śaṃkareṇa viśākhasya tat śṛṇudhvam ataṃdritāḥ praṇavam prathamam gṛtya paśvāt devam samuddharet mastake biṃdu saṃyuktam paṃcamam parigṛtya ca śivasya maṃtraḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ paraḥ mokṣaḥ paraḥ śuddhaḥ paraḥ dharmaḥ paraḥ vikṣuḥ surāpaḥ svarṇa hārīca bhrūṇa hā agurutalpa gaḥ mātṛ hā strī guru ghna śva a nyāni uktāni saṃghaśas smaraṇāt maṃtrarājasya bhasmasāt yati nityaśas sahasraśas koṭi maṃtra arjitam puṇyam labhate sādhaka uttamaḥ tri saṃdhyam yojapet maṃtram śatam ekam prayatna taḥ saṃpuṭena avaroheṇa na mṛtyoḥ vaśagaḥ bhavet jaṃghayoḥ gulphayoḥ pādayoḥ ca eva sṛṣṭi nyāsa krameṇa tu ādhibhiḥ sādhvasaiḥ anyaiḥ jvara kuṣṭha bhaya ādibhiḥ japam camānasam kuryāt divārātram ca sādhakaḥ tri kālam bhāryayā ayuktaḥ yaṃtra ārūḍhaḥ tu sādha kaḥ kuṃbha mudrām parām badhvā sukha āsana sthitaḥ pumān ātma dehe sadā adhyāyet maṃtram mṛtyuṃjayam param varṣamā ṇaṃ su dhārābhiḥ sahasra dala saṃyutam evam hi dhyāyataḥ tasya divyam rūpam prajāyate aṇima ādi guṇa avāptiḥ mānasīgati rūpavān sarvajñaḥ sūtau uvāca samāsāt vaḥ samākhyātam yat uktam śaṃbhunā āpu rā devyā aśrva kārtikeyena naṃdinā uktam ṛṣeḥ tu yat om namaḥ śivāya ṣaṭtriśe śiva saṃprīti kārakaḥ yogaḥ uttamaḥ devyaiśivena kathitaḥ parisphuṭa mudā āhṛtaḥ agastya pramukha a vipra a munayaḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ babhūvuḥ maṃtra rājena jarā maraṇa varjitāḥ etat uktam kumāreṇa vyāsasya āmi ta tejasaḥ mayā tubhyam samākhyātam maṃtram smṛtyu vināśanam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām mṛtyuṃjayoddharaṇam nāma paṃcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtau uvāca etat domesa māravyātam punar vakṣyāmi atas param hṛdayam maṃtrarājasya dhyānam japyam sadā arcanam sa ya ādi paṃca vaktrāṇi nityam saṃnihitāni yasya eva mā asti vijñānam saḥ ham na asti atra saṃśayaḥ me śubhe sidhyaṃti sarva karmāṇi aṇima ādi guṇāḥ api devī uvāca śrutam dhyānam mayā deva maṃtram saṃyataiḥ yogibhiḥ prāpyam na kadācid durātmabhiḥ kāma krodha ādibhiḥ avyākulam jagat dvaṃdva duḥkha śata āviṣṭam iṃdriya arthaiḥ su saṃyutam jagatī īdṛgvidhe deva saṃsāre duḥkha saṃjñite hi tārtha sarva matyām nām mokṣa upāyam vadasva me iti uktaḥ tām uvāca idam śṭaṇuṣva ārye yathātatham evam jñātvā acaran loke mucyate bhava baṃdhanāt dvau imau baṃdha mokṣāṇām na mama iti mama iti ca epa pāśupa taḥ yogaḥ samāsāt kathitaḥ umayā mahādevaḥ uvāca jetum rāga ādayaḥ śakyān atu janma aṃtaraiḥ api vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan tam upāyam mā evaktum arhasi aśeṣatas anāyāsena yene raṃti bhava arṇavam mānuṣāḥ tāḥ śrotum icchāmi tatvataḥ sanatkumārā uvāca tasyāḥ tat vacanam śrutvā kṛpā yuktaḥ maheśvaraḥ martyānām hita kāmāya prā ha idam pārvatīm tatas śaṃkaraḥ uvāca yadi evam mukti kāmā asi mānavānām hitā ayam vai tat śṛṇuṣva kriyā yogam kleśānām hāni kārakam yaḥ tu vāyā artha saṃyogaḥ kriyā yogaḥ saḥ ucyate evam mam kriyā yogam su saṃgatam kriyā yogam vinā āgaṃtum śaktaḥ nā eva kathaṃcana śūdra aiśvakarma nirataiḥ kriyā yoga āśritam manaḥ kārya liṃga arcane nityam mad anuṣṭhāna tatparaiḥ mad liṃga arcana śaktānām na kiṃcid bhu vidurlabham tad niṣṭhāḥ tad gata dhiyaḥ tad karmāṇaḥ tad āśritāḥ vrata upavāsa nirata ahiṃsā ādi parivarjitāḥ sattāvān sarva bhūteṣu sa rudraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ jaṃgama ajaṃgame yoma aṃve cya ātmani para tathā sama tā sarva bhūta iṣu sa rudraḥ na atra sam śayaḥ saṃprokta lakṣaṇa liṃgam kārayitvā atusthāpayet suvarṇa rajata ādyaiḥ tu satkṛtam vāsu dhātubhiḥ su pāṣāṇaiḥ sura naiśvamṭa nmayam vā api śaktitaḥ saḥ evam pūjitaḥ nityam dhyātaḥ ca eva maheśvari bhuṃjan gacchan tathā atiṣṭhan pārśva pṛṣṭhe tathā agratas jalaiḥ śubhaiḥ dhṛta ayaiḥ tunā adha anulepanaiḥ vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca eva sadā prīṇayan satatam liṃga marcayet mad parāyaṇaḥ mad kathāyām sadācittam saṃdhyāyet parameśvaram śrotavyāḥ a bhairava ādyāḥ tu kathāḥ paurāṇa saṃbhavāḥ evam samarpita manāḥ puruṣaḥ umā parāyaṇaḥ kāma anusakta puruṣaḥ umatkriyā paramaḥ param padam āpnoti jñā tvā evam makkriyā paramā bhava evam jñātvā anarodevīm ucyate bhava baṃdhanāt tat anaṃta phalam jñeyam sacā ātmānam samuddharet etena eva upadeśena tava ākhyātam mayā adhunā mānuṣāṇām hita arthāya saṃsārabha ya bhīruṇā jñāna yogaḥ tu saṃyogaḥ cittasya eva kriyā yoga stu vādya arthī dvayoḥ muktiḥ udāhṛtā kriyā yogam vinā ayogam duḥsādhyam amaraiḥ api yathā agniḥ tṛṇa jātāni daha ti anila saṃgataḥ tathā liṃga arcane bhāvaḥ udahet pāpāni aśeṣatas na vastra bhūṣaṇaiḥ ratnaiḥ na suvarṇasya rāśibhiḥ tuṣṭim yāti maheśānaḥ vinā bhaktim maheśvari iti etat kathi tat devyāḥ śaṃkareṇa purā amayā tava saṃkṣepataḥ iti uktam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi vyāsaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ vā ācarita vratāḥ anena etān pravakṣyāmi iyanena śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mama tad dīkṣayā abhiyuktaḥ tvaṃ bhūta pūrvaḥ mahā mune vyāptam hi vartate ca idam tat śṛṇuṣva yathātatham pṛthivī apaḥ tathā tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśaḥ eva ca sarvagaḥ śaśi sūryau ca śiva prakṛtayaḥ parāḥ sarve biṃduḥ nāda sthitaḥ nityam nādaśva paramātmani maṃtraiḥ taiḥ pūjyate devaḥ śivaḥ sarva mayaḥ mahān yakārasya aṣṭamam bījam mātrā dvādaśa bheditam akṣaram niratam rutvā ṣaḍaṃgam śiva mucyate dīrgha adhaṃgāḥ samākhyāta athṛd stha avakra āṇi śūlinaḥ śivasya parama atyeṣā pūjā proktā manīṣibhiḥ evam jitam liṃgam sarva kāma phala pradam jñātavyaḥ su prayatnena dhyeyaḥ sarvadā prasādaḥ ume kṛtaḥ devi maṃtra ākhyānāt maheśvari prāsāda yena vikhyātam yāsyati iha mahī tale su kalābhiḥ samāyuktam na sa māheśvaraḥ bhavet paṃca vaktvā ṇi devasya nityam saṃnihitāni ca tān ivakṣyāmi iyaiḥ matraiḥ a cyate ca iha śūlinaḥ sadyojātam prapadyāmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ dvipādau praṇava ādi samāyuktam namaskāreṇa saṃyutam vāmaḥ jyeṣṭha śva rudra śva kālarudraḥ tṛtīyakaḥ namaskāreṇa saṃyuktam dvitīyam parikīrtitam catuṣpādam samākhyātam namaskāreṇa saṃyutam sarvaṣām ca eva maṃtrāṇām maṃtrarājam prakīrtitam deva tvam mānuṣa tvam ca gāṃdharva tvam carākṣasam asādhyam sādhayet maṃtrī maṃtrarāja prabhāvataḥ striyaḥ kāśvi dākṛṣṭāḥ śataśas uparāḥ aṇima ādīn prayacchanti na atra kāryā avicāraṇā devān daityān tathā asiddhān saṃyakṣa uraga rākṣasān bhūta vaitāla paiśācān vaśam ānayet mṛtyu baṃdha ārti bhaya dam duḥkhaṃgraha samudbhavam smaraṇāt maṃtrarājasya bhasmasāt yā ati nityaśas aikāhikam hi āhikam ca saṃjvaram cāturthikam tathā aghoram nāśayati āśu darśanāt sthāvaram jaṃgamam ca eva kṛtrimam dvipam danta udbhavam nakha udbhūtam hanti maṃtra prabhāvataḥ na saṃdehaḥ svarga mokṣam ca viṃdati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām maṃtrarājaprabhāvaḥ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ evam prabhāvasya hi maṃtra rājñaḥ vidhānam uktam muninā apurāte tat brūhi naḥ sarvam aśeṣatas nyat hitāya kāle yatataḥ narāṇām vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam etat munayaḥ sametāḥ sanatkumāreṇa vidhānam uktam deśe su gupte su manoramet snātvā śuciḥ ca ekamanāḥ bhūtvā saṃsmṛtya maṃtram anasā tad aṃgaiḥ nyasam karābhyām karayoḥ cakuryāt hakāra yuktena tu vahninā paśvāt ṣaḍaṃgam guruṇā svareṇa aṣṭabhiḥ tu śikhā jñeyā aṣṭabhiḥ kavacam nyaset aṣṭabhiḥ netram uddiṣṭam phaḍustesam niyojayet māheśvaram vapuḥ ru tvā jaṭā mukuṭa bhūṣaṇam vāmadevāya jyeṣṭhāya namaḥ rudrāya ca namaḥ sarva ābharaṇa pūrṇa āgam caṃdra arddha kṛta śekharam sva śarīram tatas pūjya puṣpa dhūpa vilepanaiḥ sthaṃḍile iva api liṃge iva apaścāt yajanam ārabhet om krāṃ thṛdayāya namaḥ hṛdayam āgneyyām nyaset om krīṃ aghorebhyaḥ śirase svāhā śiraḥ īśānyām nyaset om ḍūṃ ghora ghoratarebhyaḥ śi khāyai vaṣaṭ śikhām nairṛtye vinyaset evam nyasya vidhānena hakāram vahni saṃyutam nādabiṃdu kalā ākrāṃtam aghoram hṛdaye yajet madhye ghāreśvarī devīm tasya utsaṃge tu pūjayet aṃkuśam kartarī dhvajau sa visargā aparā devī aghorā parikīrtitā ādi bījam samuddiśya dvitīyasya caturthakam trayodaśena ca ākrāṃtam vanhim ekādaśa anvitam aṣṭamasya ādimam rūpam samasta sya caturthakam hakāram tri svara ākrāṃta huṃ phaṭkāreṇa saṃyutam eṣā avidyā mahāvidyā nāmnā aghoreśvarī iti ca sakāre pūjitā devī sadyas pratyaya kārikā evam saṃpūjaye deva maghoram ghora nāśanam kapāla mālā ābharaṇam catur bhujam va ke kṣaṇam śūla dhara abhaya pradam trilocanam khaṃḍa śaśāṃka dhāriṇam dhyāyet haram yaḥ sa labheta īpsitam sarva avasthā gataḥ nityam yaḥ pūjayati śaṃkaram pratyakṣa tām iyāt dadāti abhimata siddhim aṇima ādi guṇa ātmi kām tatas prasanna tām gatvā dehena anyena śaṃkaraḥ nayati abhīpsitān lokān ja rā mṛtyu vivarjitān śrīpatra guggulasya api guṭikābhiḥ samācaret japa homam vidhānena pātāle siddhim āpnuyāt satatam yaḥ japet maṃtram aghoram kleśa nāśanam tila homena naśyam tigraha pīḍā āyupadravāḥ sadā ghore śvarī devīm yaḥ japet arcayet naraḥ yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyan triṣu lokeṣu durlabham taṃ tam prāpnoti asaṃdigdham devyāḥ ca eva prabhāvataḥ badhvā aghoreśvarīm mudrām darśayet deva tuṣṭaye tām pravakṣyāmi samyak sarva siddhi karām śubhām saṃmukhau tu karau kṛtvā sva anyonyam graṃthayā iṃgulīḥ ubha yoḥ tarjanībhyām tu saṃgṛhṇīyāt anāmike saṃmṛśya madhyam eca ūrdhvam aṃguṣṭhau śleṣayet tayoḥ kṛtvā ati adhomukhām mudrām lalāṭe sam niveśayet tatas siddhyam ti bhūta anisa deva asura mānuṣāḥ graha vetāla ḍākinyaḥ duṣṭa aśva anye sahasraśas pralayam yāṃti te sarva maitrī svacchaṃdasya mayā ākhyātam pūjanam diśi saṃsthitam liṃga iva ā sthaṃḍile vā api sarva kāma phala pradam tatpuruṣāyavi mahādevāya dhīmahi om namaḥ śivāya aṣṭātriṃśe mahādevaḥ paṃca brahma aṃtara āśritaḥ paṃcamam tu tathā avakam śṛṇudhvam eka citayā īśānaḥ sarva vidyānām īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām sadya ādibhiḥ yajanti iha yeśivam sarva kāraṇam te mokṣam āpnuvaṃti iha muna yaḥ mokṣa kāṃkṣiṇaḥ īśāna ādi krameṇa eva īśānam arcayaṃti ye pūrva va kram mayā ākhyātam ūrdhva vakram hita apasāḥ liṃga iva āsthaṃḍile śaṃbhum sarva kāma phala āptaye iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām paṃcabrahmākhyānam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhukti mukti karaḥ devaḥ śaṃkaraḥ parikīrtitaḥ vinā maṃtra ācitaḥ śaṃbhuḥ kiṃpuna maitra saṃyutaḥ jñānam mayā a muni śreṣṭha kim etat sakalam jagat jñānavān mohitaḥ daivāt mohaḥ māṃsam upāśritaḥ jānaṃtaḥ api na jānaṃti viṣṇu māyā vimohitāḥ ādyena svasya jānāti mṛtyusenā patiṣyati etat sarvam samākhyā hi mānuṣāṇām hita arthataḥ sva karma vaśa gāḥ sarve prāṇinaḥ saṃbhavati atas āhāra nidrā bhaya maithunam ca sāmānyam etat sva pada ācarāṇām jñānena hīnāḥ prabhavaṃti nityam na yat kṛtena api yathā tathā api bhāvaḥ tadā jñānavatām narāṇām bhavanti yāṃti iha punar vināśam su saṃcaraṃtaḥ bahu duḥkha khinnāḥ kṛtvā iha pāpam niraye prayāṃti paścāt tathā amānuṣa tām ku yonim stavam na kurvati yadā a svadharmaiḥ yathā jale budruvat kṣaṇāt hi paṃca brahma vidhānam tu mānuṣāṇām hita arthataḥ punar pṛcchāmi deveśa kathayasva prasādataḥ īśvarā uvāca kathayāmi śṭaṇuṣva idam sarva siddhi pradāyakam īśā nasya su bhaktānām iha amutra phala pradam kapilā paṃcagavyena snātvā jatvā aṣṭakam naraḥ juhuyāt aṣṭa sāhasram tilaiḥ mucyeta pātakaiḥ tayā udakena saṃpūrya kuṃbham jamvā śatam śatam devasya dakṣiṇā amū teḥ japet ā astamanāt raveḥ aṣṭau eva sahasram tu hutvā sarva upapātakaiḥ guggulasya guṭīḥ kṛtvā paṃcāmṛtena miśritāḥ hutvā nau vaśyā tām yāṃti yakṣa rākṣasa mānuṣāḥ jaghu āca aṣṭa sahasram tu juhuyāt samidhaḥ tatas dadhi madhu ghṛta aktāḥ tu hutvā śāṃtiḥ bhavet iha kapilāyāḥ sa vatsāya adadhi ājya madhu saṃyutam guggulam ghṛta saṃmiśram hutvā acā aṣṭa sahasrakam sarve vaśyā bhavanti iha dutvā śata sahasrakam padma ādīni nidhānāni prāpnoti mucyate tathā hatyayā a brāhmaṇasya ihaśivasā yujyatām iyāt śivāya pradāpayet paṃcagavya agniṣṭomasya tīrtha adbhiḥ sarvajātikam jabhvācā aṣṭaśatam vidvān vrajet kṣemī sadā pathi āditya abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā ūrdhvabāhuḥ śiva arcakaḥ brahmahatyā ādi pāpāni naśyati eva na saṃśayaḥ surā pānāt śarut mūtrāt steyāt sva guru dāragāt mucyate pātakāt sat yoniḥ āhāraḥ jita iṃdriyaḥ rājñām pratigṛhītvā ātu śūdra annam bahudhā atyadan gaja siṃha varāha iṣu śatru rāja kuleṣu vā manasā yaḥ japet maṃtram īśānam dhyānam āsthitaḥ dehena anena saṃsiddhaḥ prayāti paramam padam kṛtvā su duṣkṛtam devi maṃtreṇa anena mām smaret iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām aṣṭātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaṃkaraḥ uvāca gṛhītvā a dakṣiṇe karṇe ajāṃrātrau su nirbhayaḥ liṃgasya dakṣiṇāmūrtteḥ māsam ekam tu yakṣiṇī samāgatya surūpa aṭyā sarvān kāmān prayacchati karavīrasya puṣpāṇi ghṛta yuktāni juṅkataḥ nāmnā astrī vaśam āyāti samarā trāt tad agratas karṇikārasya puṣpāṇām deva gaṃdharva yoṣitaḥ samāgamya dadaṃti iṣṭam manasaḥ vatsara ardhataḥ sa lavaḥ ṇān tilān dutvā avaśam ānayate ripūn sa ghṛtena yaśaḥ kāmī sa dūrva yāyuḥ eva ca mārjanena āmayān haṃti sarṣapaiḥ akṣaṇam sadā caṃdra sūrya uparāge tu japet aṣṭa sahasrakam liṃgasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ sa kāmāni īpsitām labhet devasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ japet dā satatam sudhīḥ mita āśīyaḥ japet nityam mokṣam yāti na saṃśayaḥ sarve śmaśāneja pataḥ śubhe śāṃti kāmola bhedu tvā śāṃtiṃtu sita sarṣapān rakta puṣpaiḥ vaśe kārye kṛṣṇa pu ppaiḥ tu māraṇe vidveṣe pīta puṣpāṇi dhūmrāṇi uccāṭane tathā sarva pāpa vinirmuktaḥ śivam yāti na saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaṃkaraḥ uvāca maṃḍūkasya vasā aṃgṛtya caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamīm devasya dakṣiṇe sthitvā jatvā ca aṣṭa sahasrakam tena eva aṃjita netraḥ tu adṛśyaḥ jāyate naraḥ kusuṃbha tailam athavā apūrveṇa vidhinā akṛtam trastu adṛśyaḥ bhavati kṣaṇāt sarva jñaḥ sarva darśī ca divya rūpaḥ tu jāyate śrauta aṃjanam samādāya prakṣa pātre musamabhiḥ pidhāya havanam kuryāt kṛṣṇayā vā āsitaiḥ tilaiḥ sodṛśyaḥ pracaret mahīm tathā gorocanām gṛtya sahasreṇa abhimaṃtritam dhūpanam tena rakṣāṃsi bhūta vetāla sugrahāḥ vināyakāḥ tuḍākinyaḥ jvara apasmāra saṃbhavāḥ naśyaṃti sakalāḥ rogāḥ satyam satyam vadāmi aham śmaśāna madhyam āsthāya śavam gṛtya rujā kṣatam su saṃsnāpya gaṃdha toyaiḥ sthāpayet maṃḍale budhaḥ gaṃdha puṣpaiḥ alaṃkṛtya chādayet śukla vāsasā śave hastam samādhāya kṛṣṇām caturdaśīm anu ka pilā navanītena prakṣet aṣṭaśatam sudhīḥ iti uktaḥ śva īpsitān kāmān travīti tatra sādhakaḥ sadā tvā āpatate bhūmau niśveṣṭaḥ jāyata īkṣaṇāt kuryāt kṛṣṇa caturdaśyām japan aṣṭa sahasrakam liṃgasya dakṣiṇe sthitvā tena eva aṃgam samālabhet adṛśyaḥ jāyate sagraḥ yatheṣṭam gacchati iti ha devasya dakṣiṇāmūrtau sthitvā lakṣam japet yadi daśa aṃśena tathā aho maṃbilvaiḥ trividhā jāyate siddhiḥ viṣa dṛṣṭyā bhavanti hi jvara ādīn āmayān sarvān api kīṭa pataṃgakān brahmacaryeṇa vaimāsam paṃcagavya kṛta aśanaḥ eka liṃgam samāśritya japet mūla phala aśanaḥ bhikṣā āhāra upi ṣaṣ māsāt pratyakṣam māṃsa paśyati yānikāni ca pāpāni ghorāṇi vividhāni ca śata jāpyena deveśi bhasmasādyati nityaśas liṃgasya dakṣiṇāmūrteḥ japet aṣṭa sahasrakam paṃcagavyena ca snātvā juhuyāt ayutam punar śveta puṣpaiḥ su raktaiḥ vā apītaiḥ ca eva hi śobhanaiḥ puraścaraṇakam kṛtvā tatas sitdhyatinā anyathā kurute bhūta rākṣasān mānuṣa ādīn su kravyādān vaśi tvam na atra saṃśayaḥ kṛtvā puttalikām dhruvam maṃtreṇa anena saṃsthāpya ghṛtasya eva āhutī hunet nāmnām aṣṭau sahasrāṇi yakṣiṇī rākṣasī tathā śriyam vā api ānayati āśunā atra kāryā avicāraṇā surabhi puṣpāṇi sugaṃdhitāni aṣṭau sahasrāṇi devasya upari nidhāpayet sarvān kāmān avāpnoti śata sahasram jatvā atha liṃga mūrdhani niḥkṣipet tatas śrīḥ svayam āgatya sarvān kāmān dadāti nāgapuṣpa punnāga aśoka pāṭalā karṇikāra ādīni kathitāni sūtreṇarakṣām karoti sarṣapaiḥ sarva grahe laghubhiḥ diśām vaṃdhanam karoti sarva puṣpa abhiṣekam rutvā ātmānam abhiṣiṃcet alakṣmīm nāśayati tagara mallikā kuṃda aśoka saugaṃdhika abhiṣekena śrīḥ bhavati gatam rājyam samānayati pratipadā ārabhya sarva śukla puṣpāṇām pratidinam aṣṭa sahasram juhuyāt paurṇamāsī yā vat tatas bhavān īśvaraḥ R se kṛṣṇayoḥ kṛṣṇa yajuḥ proktayoḥ sadyojātam bhave bhava eti anayoḥ bhikṣā bhujaḥ ūvā a nirāhāraḥ vā aṣṭaguṇa sarva sugaṃdha gaṃdhaiḥ bhagavaṃtam vilipya sugaṃdha puṣpaiḥ abhyarcya aṣṭaśatam juhuyāt sa karma kurvāṇaḥ lakṣmīvān bhavati īśvaraḥ uvāca atha sadyojātena maṃtreṇa kṛṣṇayoḥ ekatareṇa maṃtreṇa tri rātra upoṣitaḥ bhūtvā aṣṭa sahasram japet puṣpa aṣṭa sahasram juhuyāt madhu ghṛta aktam yakṣa rākṣasa apsarasaḥ striyaḥ āgacchaṃti mahatīm mahatīm guggula guṭikābhiḥ raṣṭa sahasram juhuyāt aṣṭaguṇam aiśvarya bhavati atha devasya dakṣiṇāmūrtau śatru nāmnā japet atha bilvāka duṃbara aśvatthānām samidh aṣṭa sahakham juhuyāt pṛthvī rājyam prāpnoti atha vastra mālya ābharaṇa ādīn abhimaṃtrya saubhāgyam bha vati atha vaṭa adhas sthitvā śata sahasram japa iti akṣiṇī sidhyati mahā pāpāni pāpāni tathā upapātakāni tu lakṣa arddha arddha tad arddhena naśyaṃti śataśas tathā devaḥ pratyakṣa tām iyāt niṣkāmaḥ api japet evam jñānī sarvajña tām trajet svayaṃbhū bāṇa liṃge bājya utiḥ liṃge api suvrate pūrva sevām prakurvīta bhaktyā tad gata mānasaḥ śuddham pramita bhuṃjānaḥ sarva bhūta hita īrataḥ brahmacarya rataḥ maunī bhūmi śāyī jita iṃdriyaḥ sevām samārabhet yoga abhyāsena vā ayogī japa dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ pradakṣiṇā namaskāraiḥ kriyā yogena śaṃkaraḥ sarva āśramāṇām varṇānām bāla vṛddha striyām api āstikaḥ śraddadhāna śva ahani ahani bhāvataḥ dhyātvā ātmānam pratiśivam sarva bhūteṣu saṃsthitaḥ japet maṃtram tu yaḥ maṃtrī sarvam sidhyati na anyathā śivā uham jagat sthāvara jaṃgamam evam saṃbhāvayan yogī si śiva eka niṣṭhaḥ tu anuyoga dakṣaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sadā sthitaḥ asmi maṃtra jām siddhi vakṣye han tat śṛṇuṣva varānane paścima abhimukham yatra liṃgam tiṣṭhati bhāmini sthā payet dāmadevena diśāsu vidiśāsu ca paṃcāmṛta ādibhiḥ tāyaiḥ snātvā tatpuruṣeṇa vai gaṃdha puṣpa ādikam sarvam vastra alaṃkāra bhū paṇam aghoreṇa samam rutvā īśānam mūrdhni vinyaset īśānena arcayet nityam siddhi kāmaḥ iti ataṃdritaḥ mahā bhū vā deva asura pratiṣṭhitam sarva lakṣaṇa hīnam cara phuṭitam śīrṇam eva ca siddhi dam tat vijānīyāt jīrṇa uddhāram na īśānam yaḥ japet nityam liṃgam āśritya yatnataḥ nābhi mātre jale viśyam japet maṃtram samāhitaḥ samā abhijāyate dṛṣṭiḥ īśānena na saṃśayaḥ abhimaṃtrya aṣṭa sāhasraiḥ kṣipet dījāni aśeṣatas kṣīravṛkṣa samiddhiḥ tutvā śāṃtiḥ bhavet iha dehena anena deveśam vara dam sarva pāpaiḥ vimuktaḥ syāt yojapet lakṣam ādṛtaḥ go deva yoṣitām ku vātāt ku pathāt eva īśānam satatam smaret evam yaḥ vartate nityam śiva pūjā arcane rataḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca paṃcabrahma vidhānam tu yathāvat kathitam mayā sāṃpratam hi su bhaktānām tathā śuddha tapasvinām ye punar śuddha karmāṇaḥ su śuddha tapasā anvitāḥ tapasā ādi vimodate pratyakṣam devatā gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ munayaḥ ca eva satyam jānīhi suṃdari tāpasye saṃsthitaḥ brahmā anityam viṣṇuḥ aham tathā tvam tathā devi yena aham prāptaḥ bhartā su durlabhaḥ tat tat saṃprāpya teṃ devi iha lokena saṃśayaḥ sātvikam rājasam ca eva tāmasam trividham hi tat sātvikam devatānām hiyatīnām ūrdhvaretasām tām asam dānavānām hirakṣasām krūra karmaṇām su saṃpīḍya hima ātapa su duḥsahaiḥ japam dhyānam tu devānām arcanam bhaktitaḥ śubhe sātvikam tat vinirdiṣṭam aśeṣa phala sādhanam śuddha śauca ma hiṃsā tā dhī vidyā satyam akrodhaḥ udānam kṣāṃtiḥ dama udayā vāpī kūpa taḍāgāni prā sādānām ca kalpanā kṛcchra cāṃdrāyaṇam yajñaḥ su tīrthāni āśramāṇi ca dharma sthānāni ca etāni sukha dāni manīṣiṇām saṃkrāṃti viṣuva yoga ūnāda mukrāṃti yuṃjatām dhyānam biṃdu lavam recakaḥ pūrakaḥ kuṃbhaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ trikaḥ smṛtaḥ nāḍī saṃcara vijñānam pratyāhāra nirodhanam turīyam tad vadhaḥ buddhi raṇima ādi aṣṭa saṃyutam kāṣṭha avasthā mṭata avasthā haritā ca iti kīrtitā jñāna upalabdhayā uti etāḥ sarva pāpa praṇāśanāḥ nārī śayyā āsanam yānam vatram dhūpa vilepanam tāṃbūla bhakṣaṇam paṃca rājya aiśvarya vibhūtayaḥ hema bhāram tathā ātāmra graha aśva ratna dhenavaḥ pāṃḍityam veda śāstrāṇi gīta nṛtya vibhūṣaṇam śaṃkha vīṇā mṛdaṃga aśva gaja iṃdra chatra cāmaram araṃgama iti ca api enam kurute jñāna mohitaḥ jāna bhramate ghaṭi yaṃtra vat sarva yoniṣu duḥkha ārtaḥ sthāvareṣu careṣu ca kā la aṃtara vaśāya ati mānuṣya mati durlabham vyutkrameṇa api mānuṣyam prāpyate puṇya gauravāt vicitra āgatayaḥ proktāḥ karmaṇām gurulāghavāt mānuṣyam yaḥ samāsādya svarga mokṣa prasādhakam na ācarati ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ samṛtaḥ śocate ciram deva asurāḥ sarveṣām mānuṣya mati durlabham sarvasya mūlam mānuṣyam tat yatnāt anupālayet dharma mūlam hi mānuṣyam labdhvā sarva artha sādhakam yadi lābhena yatnaḥ syāt mūlam rakṣet svayam tatas dvīpānām eva sarveṣām bhujyate smin upārjitam itas svarga śva mokṣaḥ ca prāpyate samupārjitaḥ na kuryāt ā tmanaḥ śreyaḥ tena ātmā khalu vaṃcitaḥ adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvam yaḥ na prasādhayet āyuṣaḥ khaṃḍa khaṃḍāni nipataṃti tad agratas yadā an ajñāyata imṛtyuḥ kadā kasya bhaviṣyati ākasmike hi maraṇe dhṛtiṃviṃdatikaḥ tadā gṛhīta dāna pātheyāḥ mālayam yeṣām kāle yadā avāhi pūrṇa bhāṃḍaḥ puras vrajet gacchatām svarga deśasya teṣām lābhaḥ pade pade iti jñātvā naraḥ puṇyam kuryāt pāpam vivarjayet ye manāk api deveśam prapannāḥ śaraṇam śivam te pi ghoram na paśyaṃti na yamam narakam tathā kiṃtu pāpaiḥ mahā ghoraiḥ kiṃcid kālam śivā jñayā vasaṃti tatra mānuṣyāḥ tatas yāṃti śiva puram na teṣām narakāt bhītiḥ yamāt vi muni sattama iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ekacatvāriśake nu kṣātra dharmaḥ mahā phalaḥ jāti utkarṣa apakarṣa ūauca kīrtyate nṛ pravṛttaye vyāsaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇa tvam hi duṣprāpam nisargāt rāhmaṇaḥ bhavet kṣatriyaḥ vā api vaiśyaḥ vā a nisargāt eva jāyate brāhmaṇaḥ ca mu kha utpannaḥ brahmaṇaḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ bāhubhyām ūruta utpannāḥ panyān śūdra iti śrutiḥ kim utsṛtim adhas sthānāt āpnuvaṃti yatas vada sanatkumāraḥ uvāca duṣkṛtena tu kāle yad sthānāt bhaśyaṃti mānavāḥ śreṣṭham sthānam samāsādya tasmāt rakṣeta paṃḍitaḥ brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatriya tvam niṣevate jāti aṃtara sahasreṇa tamasā āviśata iyatas tasmāt prāpya param sthānam pramādyan na tu nāśayet āhitāgniḥ tathā a vidvān sa śūdra gatim āpnuyāt brāhmaṇa tvam śubham prāpya brāhmaṇyam yaḥ u vamanyate karmaṇā ayena medhāvī śūdraḥ vaiśyaḥ abhijāyate śūdra karma yathā ādiṣṭam śūdraḥ bhūtvā samācaret kurute kā sa śūdraḥ vaiśya tām vrajet yojñaḥ pāpajana dveṣṭā juvhāna śva yathāvidhi agnihotram upādāya śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriya kule jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ kṣatriyaḥ yajate yajñaiḥ saṃskṛtaiḥ rāma dakṣiṇaiḥ adhīte svargam anviccham kheta agni śaraṇam sadā ṛtu kāla abhi go brāhmaṇa ātmanaḥ ṛtha ica saṃgrāma abhihataḥ uha ve tena agni maṃtra pūta ātmā kṣatriyaḥ trāhmaṇaḥ bhavet vidhi jñaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhūtvā yājakaḥ tatra jāyate brāhmaṇa tvam su duṣprāpam rucchreṇa āsādyate naraiḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca etat icchāmi aham śrotum būhi mevadatām vara sanatkumāraḥ uvāca a gniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ yajñaiḥ iṣvā vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ iti yajña vidaḥ prāhuḥ yajña karma vi daḥ sadā tasmāt tat te pravakṣyāmi yat phalam śastra jīvinām yaḥ śūraḥ vadhyate yuddhe vimardan para vāhinīm tasya dharma artha kāmasya yajñaḥ ca eva āma dakṣiṇaḥ viṣṇu loke sajāyeta yaśva yuddhe yatra cayaiḥ kṣaṇena tāme vagatim prayati mahā āhave saṃhananam tyajaṃtaḥ om namaḥ śivāya dvicatvāri īśake adhyāye garbha utpattikam ādikam prāṇinām tat virāga artham vistareṇa prakīrtyate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe dharmasaṃhitāyām ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca śvitrāḥ saratām iha saṃsāra itāḥ tvam brūhi mama akhilāḥ atha nārakiṇām puṃsām dha man ca e iva tu kevalān śarīram upapadyate sadyas prajāyate vyam śarīram bhūta sārataḥ karmaṇā avāpi miśreṇa yat śarīram iha ātmane udbhi jaḥ sthāvara ajñeyāḥ tṛṇa gulma ādi rūpiṇaḥ kṛmi kīṭa pataṃga ādyāḥ sveda jānām adehinaḥ aṃḍajāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ unakāḥ cakrāma tsyāḥ śrca kacchapāḥ jarāyu jāḥ aśva vijñeya amānuṣāḥ ca catuṣpadāḥ tatra sikta aza laiḥ bhūmiḥ tejasā ca pratāpitāḥ vāyunā yojyamānāt khāt vīja tvam upapadyate yathartu tāni bījāni saṃsiktāni aṃbhasā punar ucchūna tām mṛdu tvam ca mūlabhāvam vrajaṃti ca tad mūlāt aṃkura utpattiḥ aṃkurāt parṇa saṃbhavaḥ parṇāt nālam tatas kāṃḍam kāṃḍāt ca prasavaḥ punar prasavāt catuṣam kṣīram kṣīrāt taṃdulasam bhavaḥ taṃdulam ca yadā pakkam sriyaṃti oṣadhayaḥ tadā yava ādyāḥ tṛṇa paryaṃtāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ oṣadhyaḥ phalaṃpāka aṃtāḥ śeṣāḥ kṣudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ śūrpa ulūkhala yaṃtra ādyaiḥ pakva aśva udaka vanhibhiḥ ṣaṣ dhā āhāra bhedena anyonya vasu saṃyogāt aneka svādu tām gatāḥ bhakṣyam bhojyam iti bhedāḥ ṣaṭ annasya madhurāya aśva ṣaṣ rasāḥ annaṃsthala āśaye pūrva prāṇam sthāpayate kramāt pīta bhakṣita māhāram sa vāyuḥ kuruta idvidhā saṃpraviśya annam adhyetu pṛthak annam pṛthak jalam jalasya adhas sacā apānaḥ sthitaḥ agnim dhamata īśanaiḥ vā yunā ādhamyamāna agniḥ ati uṣṇaṃkurute jalam karṇa akṣi nāsikā jivhā ardatāḥ śiśna gudaṃnakhāḥ mala āśrayāḥ kaphaḥ svedaḥ viṣ mūtram dvādaśa smṛtāḥ hṛd padye pratibaddhāḥ ca sarva nāḍyaḥ samaṃtataḥ tāsām mukheṣu tat sūkṣmam trāṇaḥ sthāpayate rasam rasena tenana āḍhyaḥ tāḥ prāṇaḥ pūrayate punar punar prayati saṃpūrṇāḥ tāḥ aśvadeham samaṃtataḥ tatas sa nāḍī madhya sthaḥ śārīreṇa ūṣmaṇā arasaḥ tvac tayā āveṣṭitam pūrvam rudhiram ca prajāyate raktāt lomāni māṃsam ca keśāḥ satas strāyoḥ sirāḥ tathā asthī ninakha majja asthi saṃbhavaḥ majja ākāraṇa vaikalya śukaṃca prasava ātmakam iti dvāda śadhā annasya pariṇāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ śukla annasya tatas śukrāt divya dehasya saṃbhavaḥ nirdoṣa yoni saṃsthi tam tadā tad vāyunā a spṛṣṭam strī raktena ekatām tra jet visarga kāle śukrasya jīvaḥ karaṇa saṃyutaḥ paṃca rātreṇa kali laṃbuḍuda ākāra tām jet rātreṇa māṃsa peśībhavet punar dvi sapta ahāt bhavet peśī raktam māṃsam tvacā dṛḍhā nābhi stha nāla dvār bījasya iva aṃkura utpattiḥ paṃcaviṃśati rātrataḥ bhavanti māsa mātreṇa paṃcadhā jāyate punar śva pṛṣṭhavaṃśaḥ tattha udaram ca dvi māsa abhyaṃtareṇa eva kramaśas saṃbhavaṃti hi tribhiḥ māsaiḥ prajāyaṃte sarva aṃga aṃkura saṃdhayaḥ māsaiḥ caturbhiḥ aṃgulyaḥ prajāyaṃte yathākramam mukham nāsā ca karṇau ca māsaiḥ bhavanti paṃcabhiḥ daṃta paṃktiḥ tathā guvyam jāyaṃte ca nakhāḥ punar karṇayoḥ tu bhavet chidram ṣaṣ māsa abhyaṃtareṇa tu pāyu ume ca nābhiḥ ca api upajāyate saṃdhayaḥ ye ca gātreṣu māsaiḥ jāyaṃti saptabhiḥ aṃga pratyaṃga saṃpūrṇaḥ śiraḥ keśa samanvitaḥ vibhakta avayavaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ punar masā aṣṭakena tu paṃca ātmaka samāyuktaḥ paripakvaḥ sa tiṣṭhati mātuḥ āhāra vīryeṇa ṣaḍidhena rasena tu tatas smṛti la bhet jīvaḥ saṃpūrṇasmin śarīrake sukham duḥkham vijānāti nidrā svapnam purā kṛtam mṛta śvā aham punar jāṃtaḥ jāta śvā aham punar mṛtaḥ nānā yoni sahasrāṇi mayā a dṛṣṭāni jāyatā adhunā jāta mātraḥ prāta saṃskāraḥ eva ca tatas śreyaḥ kariṣyāmi yena garbhena saṃbhavaḥ anveṣyāmi śiva jñānam saṃsāra vinivartakam evam sagarbha duḥkhena mahatā a paripīḍitaḥ jīvaḥ karma vaśāt āste mokṣa upāya viciṃtayan yathā giri vara ākrāṃtaḥ kaścid duḥkhena tiṣṭhati tathā jarāyuṇā dehī duḥkham tiṣṭhati veṣṭitaḥ patitaḥ sāgare yat duḥkham āste samākulaḥ garbhakuṃbhe tathā ākṣiptaḥ pacyate jāṭhara agninā garbha vāsāt param duḥkham kaṣṭam na eva asti kutracid dehinām duḥkha bahulam su ghora mati saṃkaṭam iti etat su mahat duḥkham pāpinām parikīrtitam kevalam dharma buddhīnām samāsa udbhavāt sadā garbhāt su durlabham duḥkham yoni yaṃtra nipīḍanāt yābhiḥ laghubhiḥ antara sthamī pat sveda aṃse ikṣu vat pīḍyamānasya yaṃtreṇa eva samaṃtataḥ śirasā ātāḍyamāna sya pāpa mudgarakeṇa ca yaṃtreṇa pīḍitāḥ yadvat niḥsārāḥ syuḥ tilāḥ kṣaṇāt tathā śarīram niḥsāram yoni yaṃtra nipīḍanāt rakta māṃsa mṛdā liptam viṣ mūtra dravya bhājanam vadana eka mahā dvāram gavākṣa aṣṭaka bhūṣitam jivhā argala anvitam bhoga tṛṣṇā āturam mūḍham rāga dveṣa vaśa anugam saṃvartita aṃga pratyaṃga aṃja rāyu pariveṣṭitam śata trayam ṣaṣṭi adhikam paṃca peśī śatāni ca sārdhābhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ channam samaṃtāt roma koṭibhiḥ śarīram sthūla sūkṣmābhiḥ dṛśya adṛśya āhitāḥ smṛtāḥ etāvatībhiḥ nāḍībhiḥ koṭibhiḥ tat samaṃtataḥ dvātriṃśat daśanāḥ proktāḥ viṃśati śvanakhāḥ smṛtāḥ pittasya kuḍavam jñeyam kaphasya api āḍhakam tam vasāya aśva palam viṃśat tad arddha kapilasya ca paṃca arddha tupalā jñeyā palāni daśamedasaḥ pala trayam mahāraktam majjā syāt ca caturguṇā śukrārddhakuḍavam jñeyam tat vījam dehinām balam raktam pala śatam jñeyam viṣ mūtram ca apramāṇataḥ śukra śoṇita saṃyogāt dehaḥ saṃjāyate yatas nityam viṣ mūtra saṃpūrṇaḥ tena ayam aśuciḥ smṛtaḥ yathā antar viṣṭhayā pūrṇaḥ śu ciḥ syāt na vahniḥ ghaṭaḥ śodhyamānaḥ hi dehaḥ yam tena ayam aśuciḥ tatas yaṃtra apya ati pavitrāṇi paṃcagavya havīṃṣi ca aśuci tvaṃkṣaṇā yāṃti kim anyat aśuciḥ tatas hṛdyāni api anna pānāni yam prāpya surabhīṇi ca aśuci tvam prayānti āśu kim anyat aśuciḥ tatas he janāḥ kim na paśyaṃti yat niryāti dine dine sva dehāt kaśmalam pūti tad ādhāraḥ katham śuciḥ dehaḥ sam śodhyamānaḥ api paṃcagavya kuśa ambubhiḥ ghṛṣyamāṇā eva aṃgāraḥ nirmala tvam na gacchati kapha mūtra purīṣa ādyaiḥ sa dehaḥ śudhyate katham śuciḥ ekaḥ pradeśaḥ api viṣ mūtrasya dṛteḥ iva spṛṣṭvā ātma deha srotāṃsi mṭat toyaiḥ śodhyate karaḥ tathā api aśuci bhāṃḍa syana virajyaṃti kiṃkarāḥ kāyaḥ su gaṃdha puṣpa ādyaiḥ yatnena api susaṃskṛtaḥ na jahāti svabhāvam ca śva puccha eva adhigacchati antarbhāva praduṣṭasya viśataḥ api hutāśanam samyak mṛd parvatena api atha bhāva duṣṭaḥ ājanmanaḥ snāna paraḥ manuṣyaḥ na śuḍāti iti eva vayam vadāmaḥ prajvālya vanhim ghṛta taila siktam
